Liaoning Agencies Implement Streamlining 57

Affected by the Soaring Gold Prices

Shenyang Correspondence: Since the soaring gold prices and the high cost of all goods, all sectors of Liaoning's political and business communities have been affected, implementing layoffs and salary reductions, and implementing austerity policies in order to save money. The Northeast Border Defense Commander-in-Chief's Office has also recently issued orders to all military agencies to lay off employees and reduce expenses. For example, the grain and forage factory and the clothing factory have all started to implement them. The clothing factory has already formulated a reorganization procedure last week by the factory director Zhao Quanxing. All the original departments have been changed to sections. The colonels in charge of the departments have been changed to lieutenant colonels in charge of the sections. The factory originally had more than 130 employees. Recently, more than 60 employees have been laid off. Those who have not been laid off have also been demoted and had their salaries reduced. The original budget of the factory was 80,000 yuan. Since the implementation of the new rules, it has been reduced to 40,000 yuan. After the grain and forage factory was ordered to reorganize and reduce its scope, all expenses must be reduced to meet the budget. It has now been stipulated that the travel expenses of the factory's staff sent to various counties to collect forage grass, which were originally 3 yuan per day, have now been changed to 1 yuan per day to save expenses.

The Northeast Transportation Committee believes that the monthly public expenses of the railways under its jurisdiction are still paid according to the original amount, and there has been no reduction, which is inconsistent with the purpose of streamlining. It has recently ordered the Beining, Shenhai, Sitao, Jihai, and Taoang railway bureaus to economize on public expenses. From July, all railway public expenses must be reduced by at least 20% compared to June. As for the temporary allowances for railway workers, they will also be cancelled from July. (July 14)

Revamping the Capital's Relief Efforts 58

The Nanjing Municipal Relief Center manages seven institutions, housing over 2,000 people. Inheriting from the former Jiangning Puyutang, it only provides care without education, and its facilities are outdated. Mayor Wei Daoming, aware of this, appointed Luo Mian as the director and instructed him to make every effort to save administrative expenses and make major reforms in the institutions. The following have already been implemented: (1) Women's Education and Care Center: The center and its branches house 800 to 900 people, living in cramped and unsanitary conditions, a veritable hell on earth. The director first selected dozens of vagrants from the vocational training center and hired workers to guide them in major renovations. All public items such as equipment, beds, and tables were neatly arranged. The practice of distributing firewood and rice was abolished, and public kitchens were established to provide meals, eliminating the idleness and dependence of the women in the center. Their abilities were assessed, and each was taught handicrafts and engaged in production and vocational work. The children they brought with them were placed in separate rooms, and children's classes were established, providing food, lodging, and recreational activities, resembling a school. The center's atmosphere has been completely renewed. (2) Infant Care Center: The old method of infant care was divided into internal and external care. External care involved entrusting the infants to rural women to breastfeed, paying them monthly wages, and sending them for occasional checkups. Internal care involved hiring wet nurses to care for several infants, resulting in insufficient nutrition and difficult care, leading to weakness, illness, and death. Director Luo has consulted and discussed with the Health Bureau to modify the nursing system. Infants will first be distinguished, and artificial feeding will be provided. Nursing supervisors and nurses will be added to the center, and many nursing students have been selected, which will be implemented starting in July. The causes of infant illness and death are also being investigated. Many are due to the fact that illegitimate children are first abandoned and abused at birth, coupled with poor feeding, making them prone to premature death. A maternity ward will be added to the center so that unwed mothers can come here to give birth to their babies, free from suffering, and to do everything possible. It will also be established in July. Other institutions, such as the vagrant vocational training center, the disabled care center, and the elderly care center, will be reorganized, distinguishing between active and passive natures, and providing different education, care, and treatment. The loan center's funds will be inventoried and reorganized, a civilian factory will be planned, and departmentalized production technology will be implemented. All of these are being planned and will soon be implemented.

Zhejiang's Disaster Relief Funds Transferred to Earthquake Relief 59

Zhu Jiahua, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Department of Civil Affairs, stated that the province has suffered major disasters in recent years, with local losses totaling no less than 17 million yuan. The number of people who have died as a result is even more uncountable. He supervised the Zhejiang Provincial Relief Association in carrying out work relief and emergency relief, but it was difficult to raise relief funds, so a disaster relief bond was issued. With the approval of the Relief Association, the department issued advance subscription vouchers before the disaster relief bonds were issued to raise cash for emergency relief. The provincial government also convened a meeting to resolve to borrow 300,000 yuan from merchants to sell rice at a fair price. However, after the wind, water, insect, and drought disasters, bandit disasters followed. Various relief measures were a drop in the bucket and did not help. Therefore, while actively treating the symptoms, they also focused on fundamental solutions. The Department of Civil Affairs formulated county and city warehouse regulations and management rules and issued them to all county and city mayors to follow. Those that had already been established were reorganized, and those that had not yet been established were required to establish them by a deadline. They were also ordered to draft estimates of revenue and expenditure to be included in the new budget for the nineteenth year as a measure to prepare for disasters. However, recently, the county magistrates of the severely affected areas reported that there was a lack of large funds for disaster relief and fair-price rice sales, and requested that the special funds for warehouse disaster preparedness be allowed to change their purpose and be temporarily transferred for disaster relief. It is estimated that these special funds for disaster preparedness amounted to more than 400,000 yuan (excluding counties that have not transferred them). Yesterday, the Department of Civil Affairs approved it. (20th)

Hangzhou Quick News 60

The Zhejiang Provincial Chamber of Commerce yesterday ordered the Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce to expedite registration because the chambers of commerce in various counties and cities in the province have been established one after another. Hangzhou City is the provincial capital, and the chamber of commerce has been established for a long time. It should expedite registration to organize a formal chamber of commerce as a model for various counties and cities. The Hangzhou Municipal Chamber of Commerce was ordered to complete registration by August 15 and establish a formal chamber of commerce.

The Zhejiang Provincial Government has formulated measures to promote the use of domestic goods. The promotion of the use of domestic goods will first be promoted by the provincial government and its affiliated agencies and staff in the province, and by the city and county governments and their affiliated agencies and staff in the cities and counties. All foreign goods that have already been purchased should be used until they are damaged. In the future, except for those that cannot be replaced by domestic goods, no new purchases should be made. The chiefs should strictly supervise to set an example.

Qian Tianhe, Director of the Zhejiang Provincial Forestry Bureau, arrived in Hangzhou from Beijing and organized an office at the Qianwang Temple in West Lake. He is actively preparing, and everything is ready. The swearing-in ceremony is scheduled to be held at the Provincial Government Auditorium on the morning of the 21st.

The Yiyao Liji Pond, commonly known as the Huitang, stretches for eighty li. The income from the pond land is allocated to education and water conservancy expenses. Now, merchants and people such as Kang Jieren are willing to pay a price of 5,000 yuan in advance to contract for reclamation and cultivation. They have submitted a request to the Department of Construction for approval.

Songjiang 61

Dispute over the Seizure of Rice Shipped for Fair-Price Sales The county has decided to start selling rice at a fair price today (21st). 36,000 packages of indica rice have been ordered, and they are being shipped in batches. Except for a small number of the first batch that has already been transported to Songjiang, the rice shops in Shanghai yesterday hired boats to transport the second batch of indica rice. The fair-price shop run by the local rice industry in this city also ordered rice from Shanghai and delivered it to the boat for loading. Unexpectedly, when passing through the Shanghai South Taxation Office, they were suddenly detained because they had recently received an order from the provincial government that they must have a passport from the Department of Finance before they could be released, otherwise the tax payable should be paid by the taxation office. The boatmen reported to the rice industry guild by long-distance telephone and asked the county government to find a way. After sending a special telegram to the provincial government, they requested that the release be ordered to maintain the people's food. No reply telegram was received. However, the number of the first batch of rice transported to Songjiang was extremely limited, and it was sold out in a blink of an eye. The fair-price shop run by the rice industry was also scheduled to open for sale at three locations on the 21st, but the rice was still on the way, so the organizers were very anxious. It is learned that the county government has prepared a document appointing Zhong Taishi, a member of the fair-price rice sales committee, to go to Zhenjiang on the 20th to meet with the two departments of civil affairs and finance, fully explaining the importance of fair-price rice sales, requesting that the taxation office be notified by telegram to release the rice first, and requesting 40 passports for transporting the fair-price rice.

Suzhou 62

Disturbances by Wounded Soldiers, Local Martial Law There are more than 2,000 wounded soldiers in the 15th and 17th rear hospitals in Suzhou. Over 200 wounded soldiers were also dispatched from Nanjing. Disturbances to shops have often been heard. The merchants and people outside Changmen have become frightened birds. Fortunately, the military police, merchants, and defense groups are closely guarded, and no major accidents have occurred. Unexpectedly, the wounded soldiers caused trouble outside Changmen again the night before. It is learned that the cause of the disturbance on this day was that more than a dozen wounded soldiers were representing their friends in negotiating with a watermelon shop on Shantang Street in the afternoon and a conflict arose. The police detained seven wounded soldiers and took them to the joint inspection office of the military police regiment. The wounded soldiers, regardless of the circumstances, were angry with the police. At 7:00 pm, they gathered two or three hundred people to go to the inspection office to demand the return of the seven arrested, but to no avail. Subsequently, dozens of wounded soldiers rushed to the Second Branch of the Second Sub-bureau of Hengma Road, snatched a fast gun from the guard post, as well as a gun machine and a bayonet, and injured two policemen, Tang Shikui and Rong Qingyuan, with iron rods. The Sixth Sub-bureau also injured Wang Xin and Sun Chengkui. A guard, Cui Dekui, was also kidnapped on Guangji Bridge. At that time, all the shops on the road closed, and the city gates were tightly closed. The authorities immediately announced a special martial law, and traffic was completely cut off in the area of Changma Road until dawn. That night, more than a dozen wounded soldiers who intended to cause trouble were also detained and sent to the inspection office. The military police authorities have telegraphed the above situation to the General Headquarters for review. The injured policemen are being treated at Suzhou People's Hospital. The kidnapped guard is still being held in the 17th Rear Hospital and has not been released. Yesterday (20th) afternoon, the inspection office specially dispatched a large number of military police to deploy defenses in the Hujiu Road area, prohibiting the wounded soldiers of the 17th Rear Hospital from visiting the road.

Provincial Committee Comes to Suzhou to Investigate Party Cases On the 16th, the party and government agencies in Suzhou seized various reactionary publications in the post office. Subsequently, reactionary suspects such as Wei Hongjun were arrested in Leyi Girls' Middle School and other places and were separately detained by the Public Security Bureau. The progress of this case has been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. It is learned that the Judicial Section of the Public Security Bureau conducted separate interrogations, but initially there were no definite confessions. Therefore, the party and government agencies separately submitted reports to the provincial government for instructions on how to deal with them. The Jiangsu Provincial Party Department specially dispatched Wang Zhilong, a member of the committee, to come to Suzhou for investigation on the 19th. After arriving in Suzhou, Wang went to the County Party Department and went to the Public Security Bureau to meet with the Judicial Section, and brought up the criminals for questioning. After several hours, because the case was serious, further interrogation was required. Member Wang has not yet returned to the province. He has now submitted the interrogation and investigation situation to the Provincial Party Department.

Wujiang 63

Three Robbers Arrested in the City At 1:00 pm on the 19th, the county's Water Police Team received a report from the investigation that bandits were lurking in the urban area. Team leader Tan dispatched police to Mingxin Tea Garden outside the North Gate and arrested Wang Jianchang, who confessed that the bandit's nest was in Xihutong next to the county government. The team was immediately dispatched and arrested Xie Pengfei and Jiang Huilai, and seized two boxes of pistol bullets and three suitcases, as well as more than 170 pawn tickets. They were immediately escorted to the team for preliminary interrogation.

Wuxi 64

Major Criminals in the Four-Life Case Escorted to the County for Interrogation and Detention Xu Jianran, a villager from Kaihua Township in the county, hired the boatman Shao Aiqiao and his two sons in March to transport a large pig to Zhejiang for sale. They were subsequently killed at Raokou in Taihu Lake, and the bodies were abandoned in the lake. The Water Police Second District has successively arrested six suspects in this case: Qian Genbao, Qian Guanbao, Wang Qiaosheng, and the main offenders Zhang Dawang (ie Zhang Darong), Yang Jisheng (ie Chen Jisheng), and Zhao Shansheng. Yesterday, Mao, the district chief, prepared a document and escorted them to the county government for interrogation. The auditor Yu opened the court for interrogation. Qian Genbao confessed that he learned that there were a total of seven people in the case, traveling on two boats. Shao Qiaosheng was stabbed to death by Zhao Shansheng with a pole. Xu Jianran was also pushed into the lake by a fugitive and killed with an iron pole. Shao's two sons were also killed. Qian Guanbao and Wang Qiaosheng were not involved. Zhang Dawang, Yang Jisheng, and Zhao Shansheng all confessed without denial. After the interrogation, Zhang, Yang, and Zhao were ordered to be shackled and imprisoned.

The three suspects Qian et al. were temporarily detained for review and handling.

Water Police Investigates Persons Involved in Opium Trafficking Last month, certain opium traffickers hired Gu Liuzi, a resident of Jiangbei, to transport a large batch of opium of 36 dan (some say more than 4,000 taels) from Shanghai to Wuxi. More than a dozen large pigs were loaded on top of the boat to avoid attention. Unexpectedly, Gu Liuzi's younger brother, Gu Kouzi, secretly reported it to the Water Police in a certain place, who carried box guns, etc., to a certain bay in Taihu Lake near Wangting and seized all the opium. Afterwards, the local newspapers spread the word and the government investigated. The County Party Department filed a complaint. It has been many days, but the truth has not come to light. Now, the persons involved in this case have been arrested by Ji Zaiyang, the captain of the Second Platoon of the Sixth Team of the Water Police Second District stationed in Wuxi, in the Eleventh District. Some opium was also seized. They are currently being interrogated.

Changzhou 65

Robbery and Injury Case in Tongshan Township On the night of the 18th, more than a dozen bandits armed with guns broke into the house of Qian Aoda in Qianjiatang, Tongshan Township, Wu County. The victim, Qian Aoda, was not at home. His wife was tied up with lead wire and forced to hand over silver dollars. She was severely injured. Her son, Jinsheng, was shot twice when he went out to call for help and immediately fell to the ground. All the cash, clothes, and decorations in the house were robbed. Afterwards, the injured were taken to Wujin Hospital for treatment, but his intestines were broken and his life may be in danger. The Changyi Steamboat Robbed in Xuantang On the 18th, the Changyi Steamboat No. 2 left Yixing for Changzhou and arrived at Xuantang, where the boat owner Gao Genyuan lived. Gao moved all the goods and money on the boat to his home late at night, intending to set sail again after dawn. Unexpectedly, six bandits came to his house that night and robbed him of more than 200 yuan in cash, 500 to 600 yuan in banknotes, checks, and foreign money, as well as clothes and decorations. The victim went to the city on the 19th to report the situation to the various merchants and intends to report to the county for arrest.

Nantong 66

Methods for Receiving Wounded Soldiers from All Circles: Nantong has established the 31st Rear Hospital. Over 1,500 wounded soldiers have already been transported there. Various local circles are discussing methods for receiving them and have resolved to establish a temporary reception center. County Magistrate Zhang has been appointed as the director. The following are divided into eight sections. There are insufficient medical officers in the rear hospital, so Hospital Director Cao, County Magistrate Zhang, and the Chairman of the Chamber of Commerce have jointly sent letters to invite medical practitioners from the four hospitals in the city and suburbs to provide treatment. More than 30 wounded officers are staying at Nantong Hospital.

Relief for Coastal Flood Disaster Issues: The riverbanks of Yao Wang and other ports in Tong County have collapsed severely. Tidal waters breached the dikes, causing widespread flooding and disaster. The Department of Construction has sent Pei Yixiang to conduct an on-site inspection. Meanwhile, telegrams have been sent to County Magistrate Zhang and Director Yao of the Bureau of Construction to consult with local French authorities and raise funds for proper relief. The county government and the bureau consider the disaster situation to be dire, with breaches exceeding fifty fathoms in width, making the engineering work substantial. A meeting of representatives from all circles is scheduled for the 22nd to discuss solutions.

Large Band of Bandits Night Attack on Wujie Bridge: The town of Wujie Bridge, located at the border between Tong and Ru, was suddenly attacked by a large band of bandits on the 18th night. They occupied the entire town and looted extensively. The police force and defense corps jointly suppressed them, engaging in a fierce battle for two hours before the bandits dispersed northwestward. In this engagement, five bandits were killed, and one Mauser pistol was seized. Three members of the defense corps were killed or wounded.

Three Counties Suppress Remnants of Pan Bandit Gang: Besides the seven or eight hundred men under Shen Guanxi of the sea bandit Pan Kaiqu's remaining forces, who have been accepted into the Jiangbei Guerrilla Headquarters for training in Yang, the remaining five hundred or so are harassing the areas of Lüsi, Pengjiatao, Hupukou, and Da'an Port. Military police from Nantong, Haimen, and Changshu counties, along with the Civil Affairs Department's police ships and the provincial water police, are currently conducting a comprehensive suppression operation.

Confiscation of Weapons and Ammunition for Local Public Use: Weapons, ammunition, and opium pills trafficked by Zhu Da have been confiscated at Yao Wang and other ports. The county government will submit a report to the provincial government on the interrogation. With the approval of the Public Security Bureau, the confiscated weapons and ammunition will be confiscated for public use and issued to the bureau for use.

Jiangyin 67

Establishment of the 25th Rear Hospital: County Magistrate Li received a telegram from Jiang Kezong, Director of the Military Medical Affairs Department of the General Headquarters of the Ministry of Military Affairs, stating that the 25th Rear Hospital was coming to Cheng and ordering the location of houses that could accommodate a thousand people. County Magistrate Li, in addition to telegramming that Jiangyin was a remote and small place and that there were too few public houses inside and outside the city, convened a meeting of heads of various agencies and hospitals yesterday (the 19th) morning to discuss all solutions. At noon, Wu Yun'an, Director of the 25th Rear Hospital, sent Medical Director Song Dingsan, leading more than 100 medical officers, stretcher teams, etc., to Cheng on the Xiangfu and Jiang'an river steamers from the capital, entering Huangtian Port and temporarily docking at Yongding Dam by river boat. An adjutant went to the county government's Public Security Bureau to make contact and looked for houses everywhere, but they were all too small and not suitable. Later, a telegram was sent to the Military Medical Affairs Department for instructions. The Xiangfu and Jiang'an steamers returned to the capital that evening. It is planned that the wounded soldiers will be transported to Cheng today (the 20th), with approximately 1,500 stones of them. The 26th Rear Hospital was originally intended to be stationed in Cheng, but now it has been ordered to be stationed in Datong.

Danyang 68

Assassination Case Occurs in Xixiang: Wu Daosan, the village head of Fengluo Village in Xixiang, rode a donkey to the city yesterday with three others, including the village chief Hu Tongqing and Zhou Heshun. On their way back to the village in the evening, they were suddenly ambushed by several bandits in Tangjia Village. The bandits pulled out pistols and fired several shots at them, hitting vital organs. The three men died instantly. By the time nearby farmers heard the alarm and rushed to help, the bandits had already escaped.

Bandits from Fengluo Village Kidnap: Yesterday at 6:00 PM, several bandits suddenly stormed into Hu Tongqing's house in Fengluo Village, ordering everyone to remain silent. They ransacked the house at will. Unsatisfied, they kidnapped his child before leaving.

Change of County Magistrate in Danyang: Wu Xiangrong, the County Magistrate of Danyang County, has repeatedly resigned to the provincial authorities and has been approved. The vacancy will be filled by Shen Yong, the County Magistrate of Qingpu County, appointed by the Department of Civil Affairs. It is reported that County Magistrate Shen will arrive in Dan to take office in the near future.

Zhenjiang 69

Citizens of Xinghua Accuse the Chief of the Public Security Bureau: Wei Zecang, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau of Xinghua County, has been accused by county residents Liu Zhenru and Ding Xia, among others, of using private individuals and abusing penalties illegally. They came to the provincial capital to file a complaint with the Department of Civil Affairs. However, after Liu returned to Xinghua, Chief Wei immediately sent people to arrest Liu. Wei personally conducted the preliminary hearing, asking whether the accusations were Liu's own idea or fabricated by others, and forced him to sign a statement withdrawing the charges. Liu firmly refused, saying that the facts of the chief's case were all there and he dared not wrongly accuse anyone. Wei became angry and detained him for eight hours before releasing him. After leaving the bureau, Liu went to the county to file a complaint about his arrest and sent his son, Liu Shuoqiang, to the provincial capital to report the accusations.

Collection of Hotel Tax Begins: The tax on hotels in Zhenjiang County was previously requested by the Education Bureau to be collected to fund education. It has been approved by the provincial government and permitted by the former University Council. The Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau temporarily collected it on behalf of the bureau, but after several months, due to opposition from the industry, the matter was submitted to the Departments of Civil Affairs, Finance, and Education for review. Now, instructions have been issued to actively proceed and not delay further. Therefore, the Education and Finance Bureaus, along with the Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau, issued a notice to hotel merchants yesterday (the 20th) stating that they will begin directly collecting the tax from hotels in accordance with the regulations starting today. Each hotel shall, from the date of tax collection, collect 5% from guests as a tax and remit the funds in full.

Yangzhou 70

Joint Military-Police Inspection Office Established: The 133rd Brigade stationed in Yangzhou recognizes that there have been disturbances caused by petty criminals in Yangzhou recently. Brigade Commander Liu specially convened a meeting of the Public Security Bureau Police Force at the County Chamber of Commerce the day before yesterday to prepare for the organization of a joint military-police inspection office. It was stipulated that the Public Security Bureau Police Force would send ten police officers and the Brigade Headquarters would send a platoon of soldiers. The Chamber of Commerce would temporarily advance 500 yuan as start-up funds. It is now learned that the office was formally established today (the 19th). The location is attached to the Brigade Headquarters. Chief of Staff Xie of the Brigade has been publicly appointed as the Chief Director, and An Zheng, the Chief of the Public Security Bureau, has been appointed as the Deputy Chief Director. They will begin operations immediately.

Education Bureau Strives to Maintain Universal Education Land Tax: The case of the Jiangdu Finance and Education Bureaus' proposal to levy an education land tax (a surcharge of two cents per tael of grain tax, equivalent to 4.88 silver dollars, with half the rate for reed fields) to compensate for the loss of the reed field universal education land tax correction was submitted to the county and then to the Finance and Education Departments. The Education Department instructed to consult with the Finance Department and submit a request to the provincial government. The Finance Department rejected the request (the reed field universal education land tax was originally under the reed field item. This land tax exceeds the original plan by eight cents. If two cents are added, the unexceeded grain fields will be exceeded). The county has now submitted a request from the Education Bureau to the Finance and Education Departments, begging to maintain the original surcharge proposal. Yesterday (the 18th), a special order was issued to the bureau, instructing it to follow the instructions of January 17 this year, jointly with the Finance Bureau, to formulate alternative compensation measures and submit them for review and transfer.

Water Police Team Seizes Smoked Opium: The Fifth District of the Provincial Water Police Team seized 1,337 taels of smoked opium. A special task force was sent from Guazhou to Yangzhou early on the 19th to hand it over to the county court for inspection. All the criminals transporting the opium have already fled.

Chun'an 71

Bandits from Jiande Invade Chun'an: Major bandit activity has been reported in the southern countryside of Jiande, causing significant disturbance in the area. The bandits have declared their intention to besiege Jiande County. Upon receiving the alarm, the Zhejiang Provincial Government instructed Regiment Commander Zhu of the 3rd Security Corps to lead his troops west to suppress the bandits. Upon hearing the news, the bandits immediately dispersed. However, a small group of them entered Chun'an via Shouchang. At dawn yesterday (the 13th), they occupied Chayuan Town, seizing all the firearms from the Chayuan Police Substation and the Chayuan Defense Corps. They also killed three policemen and one member of the Defense Corps, and wounded one policeman and five members of the Defense Corps. Shops such as Zhu Guangyu's were also looted, but the losses were not too significant. In the afternoon, they fled to Songcun and other places near Huxia. Their aim was to loot the firearms of the local defense corps. It is now reported that many of the bandits have hidden in Guocun, Yangxi Source, with their headquarters located in Qilang Temple, gathering two to three hundred people with fifty to sixty firearms. The leader is reportedly a communist surnamed Chen, who has been a primary school teacher in the area for many years. As for the 3rd Security Corps, they have all been dispatched to the Jin, Qu, and Yan prefectures. The 6th Company of the 2nd Battalion of the Corps has come to Chun'an and arrived in the city yesterday, temporarily stationed at Zhishan Primary School, and will soon be stationed in Chayuan, Weiping, and other places. The militia previously recruited by the county government (four large brigades, approximately 400 men) have all been disbanded.

Residents of Jie Village Rob the Prison in Broad Daylight: The customs of the people of Chunxi are extremely difficult and stubborn, especially in Jie Village. In the past, three villagers from Jie Village, including Xu Mao, were arrested and sentenced to fifteen years in prison for a fighting incident. Ever since they were imprisoned, there have been rumors of violent mobs coming to rob the prison. Now that the stationed troops have been transferred and bandit activity has occurred in the eastern countryside, the violent mobs believed that they had an opportunity. Today (the 15th), they gathered over a hundred people, carrying homemade guns, and marched into the city. County Magistrate Feng had no way to stop them and had to let them do as they pleased. They immediately opened the prison and released the three prisoners (as well as five other prisoners from other cases) and left together with loud cheers. Although the civilians suffered a scare, they did not suffer any significant losses.

Hangzhou 72

Hangzhou Chamber of Commerce Will Be Formally Established: The Zhejiang Provincial Businessmen's Organization Unification Committee believes that Hangzhou is the provincial capital and the Hangzhou City Businessmen's Unification Committee has been established for a long time. It should expedite registration in order to establish a formal Chamber of Commerce as soon as possible, serving as a model for counties and cities. It is now planned to combine with the Hangzhou City Businessmen's Unification Committee and set a deadline for registration. It must establish a formal Chamber of Commerce before August 15.

The Paying Agencies for Zhejiang Provincial Bonds: There are many types of Zhejiang provincial bonds. The paying banks are listed on the bond, but it is regrettable that they are not always clear. It has been confirmed that the principal and interest coupons of all matured bonds can be used to pay taxes to the county governments. In addition to receiving the principal and interest, the designated paying banks are: (1) Zhejiang Provincial Rehabilitation Bonds (Bank of China, Hangzhou, and its branch-managed treasuries); (2) Zhejiang Provincial Consolidation of Old Debt Bonds (Bank of China and Local Bank, Hangzhou, and their branch-managed treasuries); (3) Zhejiang Provincial Repayment of Old Debt Bonds (Bank of China and Local Bank, Hangzhou, and their branch-managed treasuries); (4) Zhejiang Provincial Construction Bonds (Central Bank of China, Bank of China, Local Bank, Agricultural and Industrial Bank, Hangzhou, and their branch-managed treasuries); (5) Zhejiang Provincial Highway Bonds (Local Bank of Hangzhou and its branches).

Exemption from Parcel Tax on Native Cloth: The Finance Ministry has already approved the reduction and exemption of the consumption and carding taxes on domestically produced native cloth. However, the parcel tax was still collected according to the tax regulations. The Zhejiang Parcel Tax Bureau received an order from the Finance Ministry yesterday stating that native cloth is related to the prosperity of domestic goods. Therefore, the parcel tax on native cloth should be exempted to alleviate the difficulties of merchants and comply with the government's intention to promote domestic goods.

Xiaoshan 73

Thorough Re-examination of Starting Fair-Price Rice Sales: Xiaoshan City is organizing fair-price rice sales. It has been stipulated that the Public Security Bureau will order the village chiefs to investigate and report the names of the extremely poor and the less poor so that they can be issued permits. However, recently, genuine poor households have not received permits. They have reported this to the county government verbally. County Magistrate Du believes that the purpose of organizing fair-price rice sales was to relieve the poor. If the poor cannot obtain food, it goes against the original intention. He has specifically ordered the village chiefs to conduct a thorough re-examination. If there are households that should not be buying fair-price rice, the previously issued permits should be recalled. A new list of all genuine poor people should be created and submitted for re-issuance.

Approved Surcharge on Special Water Conservancy Tax: Du Shihua, the County Magistrate of Xiaoshan County, reported that the water conservancy associations in Nansha, Anchang, and Dangshan Townships were experiencing financial difficulties. He requested the Finance and Construction Departments to levy a special water conservancy tax of two cents per mu on the land taxed under the Feng, Lao, Li, and Han designations. It has now been approved by the resolution of the Provincial Government Committee and will be implemented immediately.

Request to Borrow Autonomy Funds: The Xiaoshan County Government reported that the district offices had been established for over two months but had no funds. They proposed to temporarily borrow from the provincial tax revenue to alleviate the immediate crisis. Subsequently, the provincial government issued an order disapproving this request. Now, it is learned that County Magistrate Du believes that the county is poor and the people are impoverished, and disasters occur frequently. It is really difficult to raise autonomy funds temporarily. There is no other way than to temporarily borrow provincial funds. He has specially requested the Civil Affairs and Finance Departments to approve the temporary borrowing of provincial funds to maintain the current situation and avoid delaying progress. It is not known whether this request will be approved.

Ningbo 74

Disposal of Surplus Fair-Price Rice: The Ningbo City Yin County Civil Food Relief Committee held a temporary emergency meeting yesterday (the 18th) at 9:00 AM, chaired by Chen Baolin, due to the occurrence of rice merchants manipulating rice prices in the city. Regarding the case of how to dispose of the more than 17,000 stones of surplus fair-price rice, due to the drop in rice prices in the market, the villages are going to the rice shops to buy rice and returning their rice collection certificates one after another, the committee resolved that the city and county magistrates, together with representatives from the Party Department, would convene a meeting of rice merchants to persuade them to store the surplus rice from the committee at the original price.

Dispatch Troops to Rescue Chunhui Hostages: Chen Yuhui, the Battalion Commander of the 2nd Security Battalion stationed in this port, received a confidential report yesterday stating that Xu Zhangdong, the leader of the bandits who kidnapped the teachers and students of Chunhui Middle School in Yiting Baimahu, is now hiding with his gang and the hostages in the Siming Mountains of Fenghua. After receiving the report, Battalion Commander Chen immediately dispatched two platoons of soldiers to suppress and capture them. It is reported that they have already broken into the bandit's lair and rescued the hostages.

Raise Construction Bonds: Ningbo City Yin County has been allocated 1 million yuan for construction bonds. After repeated discussions between the city and county magistrates and the chairman and members of the General Chamber of Commerce, they immediately began fundraising. However, after a month, there are still very few subscribers, and the provincial authorities have sent several telegrams urging them. Xu Lunzhang, the Director of the County Finance Bureau, has discussed this matter with Chairman Lin of the General Chamber of Commerce and others, and plans to actively engage in fundraising in the shortest possible time. At the same time, a special appeal will be made to wealthy merchants in Shanghai to reach the fixed quota of 1 million yuan.

Anqing 75

Telegram Orders Severe Punishment of Troublemaking Wounded Soldiers: Previously, the provincial government sent a telegram to the central government requesting investigation and handling of Chen Ganqing and other wounded soldiers from the Sixth Rear Hospital for committing violence, causing trouble, and extorting money. Yesterday, a telegram was received from the General Headquarters stating that, according to reports, wounded soldiers Chen Ganqing, Xu Jinyue, and Zheng Xianghe from the Sixth Rear Hospital were committing violence and extortion outside the hospital, engaging in all kinds of evil deeds. Inside the hospital, they incited riots and beat their superiors, which was extremely illegal. The Security Department should be immediately instructed to cooperate with the 15th Brigade to go to the hospital, arrest the perpetrators by name, and severely punish them. If there is any resistance from the crowd, they are authorized to act expediently. In addition to telegramming Brigade Commander Tang, you are ordered to comply accordingly.

Letter

Xiangcheng Elementary School Letter 76

To the Editor:

Having recently read your newspaper's Suzhou news "Continuing Report on the Search and Arrest of Reactionaries," which stated that 70-80 reactionary books were found at the home of Gu Linfan (teacher at Xiangcheng Elementary School) at 35 Liu Lane, we have investigated and found that there is no such person at our school. We believe that this is a reporting error. However, as this matter concerns the reputation of our school, we are sending this special letter to correct it. Please publish it in the "Letters to the Editor" column. We pray for this. Sincerely, Xiangcheng Elementary School, July 19th.

Education News

Important News

Suspension of Sequential Supplementary Gengkuan (Boxer Indemnity Funds) 77

Countries returning the Boxer Indemnity Funds support Chinese cultural enterprises. The allocation of Gengkuan funds should be entrusted to China freely, so that the intention of returning the stolen goods is not lost. For example, when the United States returned the Gengkuan funds, the board of directors of the China Foundation for the Promotion of Education and Culture had fifteen members, with five American participants. However, the power of allocation still belonged to China, so at the sixth annual meeting held in Beijing this year, the funds for allocating and subsidizing cultural enterprises were still based on public opinion without any restrictions. Japan superficially returned the Gengkuan funds by only establishing 320 places for sequential supplementary studies. In fact, it lacked sincerity and merely used this number to buy off a portion of the people's hearts. Therefore, the Chinese members of the Sino-Japanese Cultural Enterprise Committee have withdrawn, and the government has proposed to abolish the Sino-Japanese Cultural Enterprise Agreement. In addition to requesting the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to conduct negotiations to abolish the Sino-Japanese Cultural Enterprise Agreement, the Ministry of Education has issued a special order to the supervisor of students studying in Japan, stating that since the agreement has been abolished, how can the Gengkuan quota be sequentially supplemented? The order states that the Sino-Japanese Cultural Enterprise Agreement is currently being negotiated for abolition, and all Gengkuan vacancies should be temporarily suspended from the date of the order. The names and schools of all students currently receiving Gengkuan funds should be registered and reported for record. This order.

Fourth Review Meeting of Senior High School Normal Department Curriculum 78

Passed Compulsory Subjects for Township Normal Schools

The Curriculum Standards Drafting Committee of the Ministry of Education for Primary and Secondary Schools continued to hold the fourth review meeting of the curriculum standards for the senior high school normal department on the morning of the 18th at 8:30 AM. The attendees were Ma Ketan, Zheng Zonghai, Zhu Baoqin, Zhu Jingnong, Xia Chengfeng, Hu Shuyi, Wu Yan'yin, Li Qingdong, Gu Shusen, Zheng Hesheng, Qiu Jingni, Sun Benwen, etc. The meeting was chaired by Gu Shusen, with Wang Linggen as the recorder. The matters decided upon in accordance with the ritual are as follows: (A) Educational Psychology: It was decided to delete the first article of the objectives, change the second article to the fourth article, and revise the wording to "Awaken students' interest in experimenting with various educational problems based on psychological principles." The third article was changed to the first article, the fourth article was changed to the second article, and the fifth article was changed to the third article. The syllabus, "Psychology of Various Subjects" was changed to "Examples of Psychological Research in Subjects." The minimum degree for graduation, the third article was changed to "Able to apply the psychological principles and methods learned to study various experimental problems in education." The rest are in accordance with the draft. Passing the amendments requires the consent of the original drafter. (B) Geography: It was decided that the curriculum standards for this subject would be drafted by Zheng Hesheng based on the geography of the senior high school general curriculum, with the addition of normal training materials. After the draft is completed, the consent of the original drafter must be obtained. In addition, two credits will be added to this curriculum, and two credits will be reduced from foreign history. (C) Practicum: It was decided that the original drafter should draft and submit the final version within one week. (D) Philosophy of Life: It was decided that Ma Ketan should urge the drafter to draft and submit the final version within one week. (E) Credits: It was decided to increase twelve credits for the senior high school normal department (a total of 162 credits). This includes adding seven credits for Party Principles, one credit for Arithmetic, one credit for Elementary School Administration, one credit for Practicum, and two credits for Health Education, which originally had no credits. In addition, two credits will be reduced from elective courses. Music will be increased by two credits, and Foreign History will be reduced. It was decided that (1) elective courses will be divided into arts, sciences, and fine arts, and (2) students will choose to study one of the three categories according to their interests. (G) Township Normal School Credits: It was decided to change Party Principles to twelve credits. The rest was passed. (Catalog of Compulsory Subjects for Township Normal Schools follows) (H) Curriculum Standards for Township Normal Schools: It was decided to ask various township normal schools and experts to draft the content of the teaching materials for each subject. The first item accounts for approximately 60% to 80%. The schools and experts assigned to draft each subject are as follows: (1) Chinese Language: Meng Xiancheng of Suzhou Township Normal School; (2) Social Studies: Yangzhong Township Normal School, Xizhong Township Normal School, Wuxi People's Academy, Sun Benwen of the Ministry of Education; (3) Natural Sciences: Suzhou Township Normal School, Yao Wencai of Central University; (4) Arithmetic: Baoshan County Township Normal School, Yu Ziyi, Ren Mengxian; (5) Agriculture and Crafts: Nanzhong Township Normal School, Taicang Township Normal School; (6) Fine Arts: Lida Academy, Feng Zikai, Han Tianjuan; (7) Health Education: Ministry of Health, Xu Gongqiao; (8) Physical Education: Kunqing Jia County Township Normal School, Wang Geng; (9) Music: Jiang Jingshuang; (10) (Education) Elementary School Administration: Wang Yinmin, Introduction to Education: Zheng Xiaocang, Educational Psychology: Liao Maoru, General Teaching Methods: Yu Ziyi; (11) Practicum: Nanzhong Township Normal School, Hu Shuyi.

Appendix: Compulsory Subjects for Township Normal Schools 79

(1) Party Principles, tentatively set at 12 credits; (2) Chinese Language, 30 credits; (1) Chinese language that normal students should learn, (2) Research on elementary school Chinese teaching materials, (3) Elementary school Chinese teaching methods and practice; (3) Social Studies, 27 credits; (1) Common sense of civics, history, geography, and rural social problems, (2) Research on elementary school social studies teaching materials, (3) Elementary school social studies teaching methods and practice; (4) Natural Sciences, 15 credits, mixed natural sciences, (1) Including physics, chemistry, and natural history, (2) Research on elementary school natural science teaching materials, (3) Elementary school natural science teaching methods and practice; (5) Arithmetic, 24 credits, (1) Mixed mathematics, abacus, and a summary of statistics, (2) Research on elementary school arithmetic teaching materials, (3) Elementary school arithmetic teaching methods and practice; (6) Agriculture and Crafts, 18 credits, (1) Practical rural agriculture and crafts and practice, (2) Research on elementary school agriculture, crafts, and home economics teaching materials, (3) Elementary school agriculture and craft teaching methods and practice; (7) Fine Arts, 9 credits, (1) Art appreciation and practice, (2) Research on elementary school fine arts teaching materials, (3) Elementary school fine arts teaching methods and practice; (8) Moral Education, 4 credits; (9) Physical Education, 9 credits, (1) Practice of various sports, (2) Research on elementary school physical education teaching materials, (3) Elementary school physical education teaching methods and practice; (10) Music, 12 credits, (1) Singing practice, (2) Instrument practice, (3) Research on elementary school music teaching materials, (4) Elementary school music teaching methods and practice; (11) Education, 11 credits, (1) Elementary School Administration (3 credits), (2) Introduction to Education (3 credits), (3) Educational Psychology (3 credits), (4) General Teaching Methods (1 credit); (12) Practicum, 15 credits.

Local News

National Vocational Education Conference Opens Yesterday 81

Morning Key Unlocking Ceremony at the New Site of the Vocational Education Society | First Meeting in the Afternoon

The 11th Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Education Society and the 7th Annual Meeting of the National Federation of Vocational Education Organizations were held yesterday at the French Primary School on Hualong Road. The meeting began at 9:00 AM (agenda previously reported yesterday). At 11:00 AM, the key unlocking ceremony was held at the new Society location. The first plenary session was held at 2:00 PM, followed by a dinner at 6:00 PM and a social gathering at 8:00 PM. Details of yesterday's events are recorded below.

Attendees: Ma Xiangbo, Li Shizeng, Cai Yuanpei, Zheng Tonghe, Wei Zhong, Gu Shusen, Wu Zonglian, Niu Yongjian, Yang Xingfo, Qian Xinzhi, Gao Jiansi, Jiang Zizhu, Chen Chu, Xu Peihuang, Hu Shuhua, Cai Zhengya, Liu Zhanen, Wu Hengru, Lin Kanghou, Xu Changqing, He Yushu, Shen Junyi, Wang Diancun, Municipal Party Representative Mr. Mao, Sun Zuji, Huang Jingwan, and over six hundred others.

Meeting Records: Gu Junquan, Wang Jianhou, Yang Xunxian, Pu Hua and other four gentlemen from the Shanghai Chinese Stenography Society were specially invited to take on the responsibility of the meeting records.

Key Unlocking Ceremony: At 12:00 noon, the crowd gathered at the entrance of the China Vocational Education Society to hold the key unlocking ceremony. Chairman Qian Yongming personally unlocked the door, and a group photo was taken while military music played. All members, led by Chairman Cai Yuanpei and Niu Yongjian, entered the premises.

Visiting the Achievement Exhibition: After entering the Society, the whole group visited the agricultural implement showroom, various machines, went up to the second floor to visit the office, and to the third floor to visit the work exhibition room of the administrative department, the exhibition room of the new agricultural implement promotion center, the exhibition room of the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center, the exhibition room of the China Iron Works and China Enamel Factory, the exhibition room of the experimental areas in Xugongqiao and Huangxu two rural villages, and the exhibition room of the products of the China Vocational School, Jiangsu Women's Vocational Middle School, Zhenjiang Women's Vocational School, Republic Women's Arts and Crafts School, Education Institute Practical Arts Training Center and other institutions, including agricultural and industrial embroidery, sewing, small handicrafts, and everything one could wish for, a magnificent sight. Visitors were very satisfied. Over two thousand five hundred people visited throughout the day.

Opening Address by Chairman Cai Yuanpei: Briefly stated, today is the 11th Annual Meeting of the China Vocational Education Society, the 8th Annual Meeting of the National Federation of Vocational Education Organizations, and the celebration of the completion of the new site of the China Vocational Education Society. In the sixth year of the Republic, Mr. Huang Renzhi was greatly stimulated by observing vocational education in the Philippines in the United States, and felt that the people educated in our country were learning things that were not useful and could not suit their occupations. At that time, he made great efforts to promote vocational education, organized the Society, and at the same time opened vocational schools. At the beginning of its establishment, this vocational education was discussed with more caution than it is now, so it caused a great reaction. In the educational system, in Italy and France at first there were only four disciplines, such as Theology, Medicine, Law, and Philosophy. The two disciplines of Arts and Sciences also belonged to Philosophy. Five or six hundred years ago, universities only had Theology, Medicine, and Law, with Philosophy as a preparatory course. Later, the discipline of Education was independently established, all designed for professions. Therefore, the educational system was originally designed for professions, as well as the cultivation of character and personality. In Japan, it is believed that middle schools cultivate ordinary personalities, so specialized skill courses are set up in supplementary schools for people who already have occupations to give them the opportunity to supplement what is missing in the ordinary education system. The Society examines the needs of society and professions, opens vocational schools to the best of its ability, prepares opportunities for those who will serve or have already served in the industrial and commercial sectors to receive supplementary education, and operates vocational guidance centers. In rural areas, we have carried out rural improvement work in Xugongqiao in Kunshan, Huangxu in Zhenjiang, and other places, which has been very effective. This is something the Society can take comfort in. However, due to the lack of talent and economic difficulties, we cannot fully realize what we want to do, so we have united the national vocational education institutions and have an organization of federations. This is also the result of the Society's thirteen years of efforts. Speaking of the Kuomintang's Three Principles of the People, it emphasizes the Principle of People's Livelihood. When the problem of people's livelihood is not solved, and the ideal world is not reached, and people are not happy, we must relieve unemployment. If a person cannot get a living, they will do bad things, so it must be solved. Most people in our country want to find a profession, or they have already found a profession but do not have the skills to do it. On the other hand, there are things to do but no suitable people to divide them up. (1) Leisure singing practice, (2) Musical instrument practice, (3) Research on primary school music teaching materials (4) Primary school music teaching methods and practice, (11) Education, eleven credits, (1) Primary school administration (three credits) (2) Introduction to education, (three credits) (3) Educational psychology, (three credits) (4) General teaching methods, (credit) (12) Internship, fifteen credits,

At that time, he made great efforts to promote vocational education, organized the Society, and at the same time opened vocational schools. At the beginning of its establishment, this vocational education was discussed with more caution than it is now, so it caused a great reaction. In the educational system, in Italy and France at first there were only four disciplines, such as Theology, Medicine, Law Philosophy. The two disciplines of Arts and Sciences also belonged to Philosophy. Five or six hundred years ago, universities only had Theology, Medicine, and Law, with Philosophy as a preparatory course. Later, the discipline of Education was independently established, all designed for professions. Therefore, the educational system was originally designed for professions, as well as the cultivation of character and personality. In Japan, it is believed that middle schools cultivate ordinary personalities, so specialized skill courses are set up in supplementary schools for people who already have occupations to give them the opportunity to supplement what is missing in the ordinary education system. The Society examines the needs of society and professions, opens vocational schools to the best of its ability, prepares opportunities for those who will serve or have already served in the industrial and commercial sectors to receive supplementary education, and operates vocational guidance centers. This is something the Society can take comfort in. However, due to the lack of talent and economic difficulties, we cannot fully realize what we want to do, so we have united the national vocational education institutions and have an organization of federations. This is also the result of the Society's thirteen years of efforts. Speaking of the Kuomintang's Three Principles of the People, it emphasizes the Principle of People's Livelihood. When the problem of people's livelihood is not solved, and the ideal world is not reached, and people are not happy, we must relieve unemployment. If a person cannot get a living, they will do bad things, so it must be solved. Most people in our country want to find a profession, or they have already found a profession but do not have the skills to do it. On the other hand, there are things to do but no suitable people to do them. This requires vocational education to teach them the skills so that they can do things, have food to eat, and cultivate talents so that society has useful people. This responsibility is very heavy, so the Society must work hard to complete the task. Today, in the members' meeting, the director of the administrative department will report on the Society's affairs, and the chairman of the National Federation of Education Institutions will report on the Association's affairs. I hope everyone will give guidance.

Speech by Ma Xiangbo: Briefly stated, Liezi has a saying: "In Qi there are national scholars, in Song there are physiognomists. The national scholars are rich and the physiognomists are poor. The physiognomists went to Qi to ask the national scholars for the art of getting rich. The national scholars told them that getting rich lies in stealing. The physiognomists then returned to their country and committed theft. Soon they were exposed and imprisoned. Then they questioned the national scholars, who then told them that gold, jade, and wealth are private property and cannot be stolen. Only public property can be stolen." My view of science is that it is stealing, and it is exactly the same as the national scholars of Qi. What is stolen is the wind, rain, dew, and water of the world. He can use steam power and electricity. Speaking of whether everyone should have a profession, I think a person who cannot support themselves or support others is a thief. Everyone should have the strength to support themselves and to support others. The Chinese like to be closed off. In the imperial era, the Society was performing tricks in front of the emperor. Everything was just individual, there was no public. So China is an individual country. In fact, the country belongs to the people. Everything in the world, no matter how big or small, is created by the ten fingers of mankind. People are born to have professions. Americans believe that anyone who does not work should not eat, should not be allowed to eat. To truly treat the people as people, they must have a profession. Only by being able to do a profession can they live up to the grace of heaven and earth in giving birth to people. If everyone can have this spirit of vocation, the Republic can flourish. So to flourish, we need the spirit of vocation, we need progress, not like people suffering from jaundice. We must work for the benefit of the country, the race, and mankind. This is true vocation, true humanity.

Speech by Niu Xisheng: Briefly stated, vocational education is very important. In a country, if the people have no profession, it is equivalent to having no people. Therefore, we must use the spirit of mutual assistance to seek the common survival of each other's careers in order to succeed. Small businesses, one's own body and family, and large businesses, the country, and the world can all be started. If there is no profession, how can it be developed? Therefore, everyone must work practically to solve various problems. The Society, at a time when people did not pay attention to it, saw the importance of vocational education and started working, so it has achieved today's success. This is worthy of admiration. Now that everyone knows the importance of vocational education, we should make further efforts to not only solve the problem of profession but also solve the problem of education, so as to create a great career for the world and mankind. Please widely publicize the importance of vocational education to those present to achieve success. China's livelihood lies on this one line.

Report from the Administrative Department: Director Jiang Wenyu reported, as did Wang Cheng, the chairman of the National Federation of Vocational Education Institutions for the year, and the dean of the Agricultural College of the Central University. Details are omitted.

Speech by Gu Yinting from the Ministry of Education: Briefly stated, the National Government attaches importance to the Three Principles of the People education. The Three Principles of the People emphasize the Principle of People's Livelihood, which is related to vocational education in every way. This is something that needs to be discussed by experts. I hope the Vocational Education Society will study it for reference. The Ministry of Education plans to compile a curriculum for home economics in the near future. I hope to draft it to promote its early completion. The scope of education is very broad. The administrative organs cannot take care of everything. I hope you can provide materials. In addition, I have a few contributions: (1) The center of foreign vocational education is in vocational supplementary schools, training lower-level industrial talents, which is practical. We must also take this vocational supplementary education as the center and start from it, then there is hope. (2) China is an agricultural country, but ordinary schools do not pay attention to it, so the Society should pay attention to agricultural education. If it can be done well, there will be many avenues for students. (3) Women's management of household affairs is the case in all countries. The Society should pay special attention to discussion for the reference of administrative organs. (4) Vocational guidance, all countries have special institutions or commissioners to manage it, which shows its importance. The Society has already established such an institution, and should continue to work hard in the future.

Speech by Yang Xingfo: Briefly stated, since ancient times, there have been no people who eat without working. But why are there so many people who eat without working now? It can be thought of how many people work but cannot eat. If this problem is not solved, the Principle of People's Livelihood will not achieve its purpose. Therefore, what we advocate vocational education is to advocate eating education. In the current era of the recession of industrial institutions, not to mention others, even the educated people above the middle class should do some farming and work to realize the Principle of People's Livelihood. A Chinese saying goes, "Everyone sweeps the snow from their own doorstep, and does not care about the frost on other people's roofs." I will now change it to "Everyone produces their own clothes and food, and does not care about the beauty and goodness of others." If everyone can support themselves, this is true beauty and goodness. Therefore, I want to focus on profession and not on occupation.

Speech by the representative of the Municipal Party Department, Mr. Mao: Briefly stated, China's past education had three defects: 1. Inequality of opportunity, 2. The textbooks for the aristocracy were classical or profound, so the common people could not receive education. Therefore, we must enable farmers and workers to have education, and we must promote vocational education. The Principle of People's Livelihood in the Three Principles of the People emphasizes the construction of industry and labor protection. With the achievements of vocational education, everyone will have something to support themselves. Therefore, vigorously promoting this kind of education now is suitable for the actual situation of Chinese society and helps the progress of the Principle of People's Livelihood to achieve the ultimate goal.

Speech by Lin Kanghou: Briefly stated, although people have two hands that can do things, they must have a business for them to do. Foreign businesses are very developed, but in China, businesses are gradually decreasing, so they are increasing day by day, so even if they have hands, they cannot move. Therefore, we must think about how to develop the industry and first promote the three educations.

First Plenary Meeting in the Afternoon 86

Amending the Society's Constitution: The first plenary meeting was held at the French Primary School at 2:00 PM. Those who attended were the same as in the morning. Wang Kecheng and Liu Zhanen were elected as chairmen. Yang Weiyu then reported: (1) Tomorrow at 6:00 PM, the China Science Society, China Enamel Factory, Shanghai Hujiang Tongji Guanghua Great Xia and other sixteen groups will host a welcome dinner at the New New Restaurant. Admission is by invitation. (2) Today at the Wood Society, there will be a dinner at 6:00 PM. Those interested in joining should join on time. At 8:00 PM, there will be a social gathering with the Drama Association performing "The Merchant of Venice". Then, Mr. Jiang Wenyu reported that the motions were divided into four categories for discussion: (1) General Vocational Education Group, (2) Agricultural and Rural Vocational Education Group (3) Industrial and Commercial Supplementary Education Group, (4) Vocational Guidance Group, then Yang Weiyu reported on the amendment of the Society's constitution, which was immediately opened for discussion (1) Article 3, Category 3 Jiang Wenyu proposed to change the word "Department" of Vocational Guidance Department to the word "Institute" Liu Zhanen seconded and passed (2) Article 5 Jiang Wenyu proposed to amend Liu Zhanen seconded and passed (3) Article 7 should be held once every two years in April, there is a need to amend the words "April", it is proposed to change it to July or August (20 people supported) Liu Zhanen advocated that it should be held in April and should not be deleted. Huang Li proposed to change it to the summer vacation, 29 supporters passed, (4) Huang Renzhi Jiang Wenyu explained the reasons for proposing to delete Article 12, passed, (5) Change Article 13 to Article 12, and so on, passed (6) Jiang Wenyu proposed that the words "Annual General Meeting" in Article 17 should be changed to "Members", Huang Li seconded and passed (7) Li Bohan proposed that the members' meeting should be held once every two years, it is proposed to change it to one year Chen Liangeng Huang Li advocated two years, slightly passed,

Members expressed their opinions (1) Wang Diancun said that vocational education has gone through the stages of advocacy, research, and implementation. In the past, schools trained talents, and everyone suffered from learning things that were not useful. It is best to break the school style and allow students to practice in factories or schools to set up factories to let them work. There is no distinction between workers, businessmen, farmers, and students, and they are integrated to avoid estrangement. In recent years, the production skills of students in schools are far inferior to those of factory apprentices. This is because the failure of training is a major reason, and the inappropriateness of the curriculum is also the conclusion. Because the national uniformity is too rigid and boring, those who choose subjects should also pay attention to the vocational courses in ordinary middle schools and should be given more flexibility. I hope that the Association will request for corrections.

It was decided to divide into groups for discussion: the first group Liu Zhanen Jiang Wenyu General Vocational Education Group, the second group Zhu Kecheng Yao Huiquan Huang Qisheng Rural Education and Agricultural Education Group, the third group Yang Weiyu Zhao Shifu Industrial and Commercial Supplementary Education Group, the fourth group Zheng Xigu Wang Diancun Pan Yangyao Vocational Guidance Group. Discussions will be held separately from 8:00 AM today and will be decided at the plenary meeting in the afternoon.

Free discussion: Mr. Zheng Tonghe said that there are three mistakes in vocational schools: (1) too much emphasis on form and not practical needs; (2) those who run vocational schools are inconsistent with the industrial sector and go their own way; (3) most of the students entering vocational schools now are those who failed to be admitted to other schools. To remedy this, first, the school format should be broken, and there is no limit to how many years to graduate, depending on their level. Second, they should contact or form a committee with the industrial sector to discuss it. Third, do not let young people enroll at will. Fourth, all occupations can be trained, even apprentices may be accepted and taught the knowledge of apprentices. Sun Zuji, Huai Boming, Li Lubin, Zhang Luquan, Yan Xiaofan, and others also discussed.

Dinner and Social Gathering: A dinner party was held at 6:00 PM and a social gathering was held at 8:00 PM. The drama association performed a play, and more than a thousand people watched.
