A Laughing Matter 97

Man: Don't dislike that I'm old. You really should marry a fifty-year-old man. That way, he can protect you anytime, anywhere.

Woman: Rather than marry a fifty-year-old man, I'd rather marry two twenty-five-year-old men. Wouldn't they protect me even more thoroughly with one on each side?

Man: I really love you to the extreme. Everything I have is yours. I'm willing to offer the whole world at your feet.

Woman: You're clearly talking nonsense and trying to trick me. May I ask, is the whole world your private property?

Wife: Last night, we weren't having any fun at the dance party, so I came back to sleep first.

Husband: But as soon as you left, my fun began.

Diner: Do you feel bored serving people every day?

Waiter: Nothing else, but waiting for the tip is the most boring part.

Rich man: You owe me fifty dollars. To this day, the principal and interest are nowhere to be found. When will you be able to return it to me?

Poor friend: I pray here every day that you live past a hundred years old, so that I may have a day to pay you back this debt.

Postscript to the Opening of the National Joint Commercial Center 98

Sun Choucheng

On the 16th of the month, the China National Joint Commercial Center held its opening ceremony. The details have been reported in this newspaper. Now, I will record some trivial things I saw and heard for the Free Talk section. I think it will also be welcomed by those who advocate for national goods.

Guests Receive Gifts On the day of the event, the venue was the large assembly hall on the upper floor of the old Municipal Hall on Nanjing Road. There were thirty-six rows of seats for guests, each row able to seat thirty people. The walls were covered with slogans such as "Promoting National Goods Can Recover Rights and Interests," "Strive for the National Goods Movement," and "Promoting National Goods is the Solution to China's Livelihood Problems." Hundreds of Party and National flags were hung in the air. After guests signed in, they were led to their seats by ushers and given a towel from the Samsung Cotton Mill, a pair of artificial teeth from the China Rubber Factory, and a package of Western-style pastries from Guanshengyuan.

Sun Yat-sen Visits the Municipal Hall for the First Time The place where foreigners handled political affairs in the Public Concession was rarely visited by our countrymen. The interior layout was entirely Europeanized. On the day of the event, a platform was built high in the hall, with a full-body portrait of Sun Yat-sen woven by the Du Jinsheng Silk Weaving Factory, about four feet long, wearing a Zhongshan suit. Next to it were Party and National flags in a crossed shape. A gentleman sitting next to me said that this place was the meeting place of the governing bodies of the eighteen nations. There had never been a portrait of Sun Yat-sen. Today, to be able to hang an embroidered portrait on the stage can be said to be Sun Yat-sen's first visit. The listener burst out laughing.

Zhang Zilian is Exceptionally Modest The National Joint Commercial Center was initiated by Zhang Zilian, the manager of the Samsung Factory. On the one hand, he rented the house from the landlord Hardoon. On the other hand, he invited enthusiastic advocates for national goods to serve as members of the collection, design, and publicity committees, and they proceeded separately. On the day of the event, when Zhang reported on the preparations, he attributed the success to the support of various organizations and comrades, as well as the enthusiastic participation of various manufacturers. He also said that he hoped that all the gentlemen who attended would provide detailed guidance so that he could inherit their intentions and strive to carry them out. His words were quite modest.

Wang Yansong's Words are Experienced When Wang Yansong represented the Municipal Party Department to deliver a speech on the day of the event, in addition to detailing the flooding of foreign goods and saying that if national goods were not promoted, rights and interests would inevitably overflow and it would be too late to regret, he also said that Nanjing Road is the most prosperous place for commerce in Shanghai. Organizing a national joint commercial center here is related to the observation of foreigners and should be especially cautious. He hoped that all manufacturers participating would select fresh and timely, cheap and good-quality goods for display and sale.

Absolutely do not fill with stock, leading to the loss of enthusiasm of the main customers. Mr. Wang is an old manager of the Daxin Silk and Satin Bureau and understands the commercial situation. What he said was indeed an experienced talk. Everyone was pleased.

Minister Kong Bows His Head on Stage Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Industry and Commerce, personally attended the meeting and delivered a speech on the day of the event. When he went on stage, the glass window above the ladder was installed too low. He was a tall and burly man, and if he had entered upright, he would have bumped his head. Therefore, the receptionist asked him to bow his head up the ladder. He obeyed and went on stage, smiling cheerfully. In his speech, in addition to discussing whether the development of national products was related to the national economy and the people's livelihood, he also said that the national commercial factory organized this time has the three advantages that Mencius called "Heavenly Time, Geographical Advantage, and Human Harmony." He hoped that this would be extended to the whole country to save rights and interests.

Random Notes from a Trip to Hangzhou (Part 2) 99

Huang Jiping

Chen Bulei, Director of the Zhejiang Education Department, hosted a dinner party for me and others at the residence of Huang Shufen one night. He was humble and amiable, not losing the character of a newspaper reporter. He spoke eloquently about the plans to reorganize education in Zhejiang Province, which were quite important. He also asked Ge about the current situation of the Shanghai press, as he had not forgotten his former career. During the dinner, the Ninghang Highway was discussed. This road spans the two provinces of Jiangsu and Zhejiang and is sponsored by the construction departments of the two provinces. It has been under construction for more than a year and is about to be completed. Chen said that he had traveled with Chairman Zhang Jingjiang by car from Ningbo to Hangzhou. The road was quite straight, but the bridges had not yet been completed. It will be officially open to traffic soon. I only think that the bandit atmosphere in the Liyang and Yixing areas is not suppressed, and passengers may have to stop.

From my observations in Hangzhou for several days, I deeply feel that after the failure of the silk industry, commerce has been greatly hit, and many people have lost their jobs. The society presents a rather panicked phenomenon. Hangzhou has always been known for producing silk in large quantities, and finance has been used to circulate it. The people's livelihood has been able to develop. In recent years, silk factories have gone bankrupt one after another, and weavers have suffered the pain of unemployment. Sixty or seventy percent of the rickshaw pullers in Hangzhou were weavers in the past. A rickshaw puller told me that when they were weavers, they could earn more than 20 yuan to 40 yuan a day. To look after a family, there was still a surplus. Now, running around all day only seeks to be full. His words were very sad. Consider the reasons for the failure of the silk industry: (1) The heavy collection of exorbitant taxes and levies. (2) Failure to improve fabrics. (3) Popularity of rayon. (4) Chinese people compete to pursue foreign goods. In view of this, the government, silk merchants, and the public are all responsible for a part of the responsibility. Are those who care about the industry also aware of the failure of the silk industry and know how to find ways to remedy it?

The night before leaving Hangzhou, a gentleman from the Asian Walking Group visited Ge and reported on the progress of the walk between Shanghai and Hangzhou. According to him, "From Shanghai to Hangzhou, walking along the railway, a minimum of fifty li and a maximum of one hundred twenty li per day. We arrived in Hangzhou in six days. Near Jiashan, we were stopped by the road police. We showed our passports and were allowed to pass. When approaching Jiaxing, it was getting late. We encountered several bandits dressed as farmers, who threatened us with weapons and searched us thoroughly. The eighty-five yuan we were carrying was all taken away. Later, we told them about the purpose of our walk and begged them to return half of it to cover our food and lodging expenses on the way. After much negotiation, they gave us a few odd coins and fled." Huang Jun is quite capable. He said that the male and female comrades in the group vowed not to marry. This trip is scheduled for six years. You can return to your hometown. His perseverance and heroic spirit are truly rare.

Random Talk in the Midst of Expensive Gold Yan Rongtang 100

Since the price of gold has skyrocketed, it has greatly affected our country's business community, which is based on silver. Now, I will select and write down the main things I have seen and heard, as follows.

Eastern Travel Impressions (13) Qian Hua 101

In addition, Tokyo Performing Arts Communication specializes in recording films, dramas, and music. There are also International Film Communication, etc. Providing current affairs photos and copper plates are Nikkan Photo Communication, News United Press, Dentsu, and Jiji Photo Express News Agency, among several others. The most prestigious newspaper is the Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun, which is a branch of the Osaka Mainichi Shimbun. Its daily circulation ranks first among Tokyo newspapers. Last New Year's Day, it broke the one million copy record. To date, the highest point reached 1.11 million copies. The next is the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun, a branch of the Osaka Asahi Shimbun. Its daily circulation is several hundred thousand copies. Next is the Jiji Shinpo, with a capital of 1.25 million yen, the Kokumin Shimbun with a capital of 3 million yen, the Chugai Commercial Shinpo with a capital of 2 million yen, and the Hochi Shimbun with a capital of 1.1 million yen. The president is Marquis Okuma, and it is the organ newspaper of the Minsei Party. Tokyo is the birthplace of the Japanese newspaper industry, with a longer history, generally around sixty years. The oldest is the Tokyo Mainichi Shimbun, founded in the third year of the Meiji era (60 years ago). It is individually operated with a capital of 500,000 yen. Because its foundation is solid, it has a considerable position. However, later, because Tokyo's productivity was far inferior to Osaka's, the Osaka Asahi and Mainichi newspapers rose sharply, surpassing their predecessors. Furthermore, they gradually expanded outwards with their economic power. Initially, Mr. Murayama Ryuhei, the president of the Osaka Asahi Shimbun, began operating the Tokyo Asahi Shimbun in the 21st year of Meiji, forming a strategic alliance with the Osaka Asahi, exchanging information. In just a few years, the voices of the Eastern and Western Asahi newspapers greatly resonated. Later, the Osaka Mainichi rose sharply, but felt the pain of being a lone army without support. It actively sought newspapers in Tokyo to cooperate with. In February of the 44th year of Meiji, it implemented the acquisition of the Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun, and then made vigorous reforms, giving it a new look. The Tokyo Nichinichi Shimbun was founded in the 5th year of Meiji and had a reputation in society. Through the cultivation of the Osaka Mainichi, it has risen to the top position today. Therefore, when talking about today's newspapers in Tokyo, the first to be mentioned are the Tokyo Nichinichi and the Tokyo Asahi. But in reality, it is still the competition between the Osaka Mainichi and Asahi. The public opinion of the entire Japanese nation is controlled by these two newspapers, which is indeed enough to be proud of. As for newspaper studies, Tokyo is the center. The most famous is the Shinbun Kenkyujo (Newspaper Research Institute), which specializes in the training of newspaper reporters. Publications include "Newspaper" and "Newspaper Reporter" (daily), "Japan Newspaper Yearbook," etc. Furthermore, based on the International Conference of Newspaper Experts, it increased the education of newspaper reporters. On October 1st of last year, it established a newspaper research room at the Tokyo Imperial University, with professors from the Faculty of Literature, Faculty of Law, and Faculty of Economics responsible for guidance. Three students were selected from each of the three faculties to engage in research. The research materials focus on the history of newspapers and investigations of foreign newspapers, etc., for a period of one year. It is expected that the results will be considerable. In addition, various companies have dozens of publications on newspapers, such as "Collection of Advertising Theories," "Newspaper Chronology," "Newspaper and Society," and "Collection of Laws and Regulations on International Publishing Relations." The development of the Japanese newspaper industry has unlimited potential.

The price of gasoline used in automobiles (commonly known as "gasoline") has risen from 55 cents per gallon to 60 cents, then to 85 cents, and recently it sells for over $1.10. However, according to a Westerner named Lao Baiqi, the cost of this gasoline is very low, but due to transportation, it reaches such a high price. Previously, Standard Oil had investigated various provinces in China, with the Sichuan oil fields being the best. If refined scientifically, its quality would surpass that of all current brands. It was originally intended to set up a factory in Shu, but the proposal was abandoned due to opposition. When I (the Westerner referring to himself) traveled to Sichuan, I saw the local people digging for oil to use for lighting. Such a great treasure trove, yet no one in China has risen up to exploit it to meet the needs of the people. It is truly laughable. Alas, the Chinese economy is heading towards panic, mostly due to internal strife. However, the daily loss of huge amounts of resources is also one of the reasons.

Recently, various notices of price increases for domestic goods have frequently appeared in the newspapers. Judging from their tone, they are all due to the increase in the price of raw materials. However, since they are called domestic goods, their raw materials should also be produced in our country. If there are already such materials in the country, then efforts should be made to improve them. If not, then a survey should be conducted throughout the country to see if there are such raw materials. If there are, then start exploiting them. If not, then a way must be found to replace these raw materials with other things. Only in this way will we not be controlled by others, and the rise and fall of gold prices will not matter much. It is hoped that all those engaged in domestic goods will pay attention to this point as soon as possible.

Foreigners' enthusiasm for using domestic goods is something that Chinese people cannot match. Here is an example to illustrate this and serve as a warning to the Chinese people. The director of the Shanghai Post Office was originally a person from a certain country. During his tenure, everything he needed was produced in his own country. Later, he was replaced by another person from a certain country. After arriving at the bureau, he gradually changed to using goods from his own country. Even something as small as a pen nib had to be replaced. Chinese people, reading this, should be enlightened.

Warmth in the Heart (337) Bao Tianxiao 102

Chapter 12: Farewell Banquet, Leaving Wine, Plucking Flowers to Leave a Beautiful Impression, Garden Gathering, Tea Tasting to See Beautiful Appearance

That tea tasting place... did not have any noble ladies or virtuous women. Several old tea servers from Zhang Garden were still on duty there. Because there were fireworks and other after-dinner entertainment in the evening... they were set off on the lawn there. Therefore, there were many people sipping tea here. Originally, the tea sipping place was in An Kai's brother's place. Now, An Kai's brother's place has become a playground for various games. So the tea sipping place was moved to this lawn. Special five-colored electric lights were installed, reflecting in the dense trees and forests... making it even more brilliant and spectacular. When Long Ziyun and Zuo Shichen arrived here... they saw that the tea sipping place was already full of people... with hair ornaments shimmering, clothes fragrant, and the sound of pearls and jade chattering... Fortunately, there was still an empty space... and the tea server recognized Zuo Shichen. He said... Mr. Zuo, sit here... If you were any later, there wouldn't even be this seat. Zuo Shichen and the others had to sit down. It was originally a movable table... with a white tablecloth on it. Several rattan chairs were placed haphazardly. The tea servers went to brew two pots of tea. In the past, one pot of tea could be shared by two people... but today it was stipulated that each person had one pot... just to teach the tea drinkers to brew more pots, to produce more pots... to produce more tea money... After settling down... Long Ziyun asked the tea server... Isn't there fireworks today? The tea server said... Yes... that's why it's so lively here... Long Ziyun said... Are the fireworks going to be set off soon? The tea server said... It won't be until 11:30... If they were set off earlier... people would leave after watching the fireworks... So it's better to wait a little longer. Today there is a special kind of Eastern fireworks... that are very high. When they reach the sky... they release five-colored planets... ...... While the tea server was speaking enthusiastically... Zuo Shichen suddenly heard a laughing voice behind him. It seemed very familiar... At this time, Long Ziyun had already noticed it... and said to Zuo Shichen in a low voice... The one behind you. The one wearing a parrot green shirt... doesn't she look like Ruiyun? Zuo Shichen hurriedly turned his head... and it was indeed Ruiyun... He saw that there were six or seven women... sitting around a round table... as if they were holding some kind of round table conference... There were middle-aged women in their forties... and young girls of thirteen or fourteen... The other young ladies of sixteen, seventeen, eighteen, and nineteen, and Ruiyun were evenly matched... There were four or five of them... and everyone was talking and laughing... When Zuo Shichen turned his head... Ruiyun had already seen Zuo Shichen... Looking at her, she seemed to be stunned for a moment... and hurriedly avoided Zuo Shichen's gaze. She was talking and laughing with a young lady next to her who had bangs on her forehead and a braid. When Zuo Shichen didn't look at her... she was secretly watching the shadow of Zuo Shichen's back... Zuo Shichen didn't see it... but Long Ziyun, who was sitting opposite Zuo Shichen, saw it very clearly... It was indeed:

Helplessly, the flowers fall... It seems like familiar swallows return...

If you want to know what happens next, listen to the next chapter...

Silk and Tea: The Silk Market Remained Lifeless Last Week 110

European sales are increasingly sluggish... Japanese silk factories are preparing to shut down.

Silk prices are high, market prices are low... Chinese silk merchants cannot sustain themselves.

Last week, the local foreign silk market had already become despondent. Since the changes in the overseas market and economic sector, the commercial market has been declining daily. The sounds of factories reducing work and stopping machines are rising, and the number of unemployed workers is increasing daily. Silk weaving factories in New York, Lyon, and England are taking advantage of the summer vacation period to temporarily suspend work. Even if they resume work after the vacation, they are all preparing to increase the use of rayon to reduce costs and maintain the current situation. The need for raw silk is decreasing, and there is still a thick stock of silk, sufficient for more than two months of raw materials. The raw silk market has no vitality in silk factory sales, silk prices continue to fall, and there is a market with no transactions. Futures silk trading has completely stopped. Silk exchanges in New York, Lyon, Yokohama and other places are also observing the summer vacation, and futures silk trading has stopped auctioning. The future of the silk market is becoming increasingly critical. Japanese silk factories are now preparing to shut down in order to reduce silk production and are requesting the country's government to provide low-interest funds for relief. However, Chinese silk merchants are selling at a loss due to high silk costs and low market prices, and there are few buyers, so they will be unable to sustain themselves. Last week, silk sales almost stagnated, and transactions were limited. Currently, 700 to 800 bales of silk are being exported. Overseas Chinese silk prices continue to decline. The Municipal Executive Committee Cables Request for Strict Punishment 111

Of Participants in the Expanded Conference

The Municipal Executive Committee cabled the Central Executive Committee yesterday, saying, "In this time of national crisis, Nanjing Central Executive Committee, in view of the unfavorable situation on the front lines and the disintegration of internal organization since Yan and Feng declared their rebellion, suddenly conceived a fanciful idea, gathered all kinds of reactionary elements, and called for their so-called expanded conference of central cadres, confusing rumors and stealing names. Although they gathered substitute signatures, the meeting was not a meeting, and in the eyes of knowledgeable people, it was not worth a laugh, and there was no value or effect to speak of. However, it is heartbreaking that the opportunistic elements participating in such illegal meetings are betraying the Party with wild ambitions, following the stench like mosquitoes and flies, and changing their minds rashly. Although these people may have worked hard in the revolution in the past, their rebellious actions are now obvious, and their crimes cannot be forgiven. We should ask your committee to investigate and punish them separately, either by expelling them from the Party or by issuing arrest warrants, in order to maintain Party discipline and eliminate reactionaries. We eagerly await your orders." Sincerely, the Shanghai Special Municipality Executive Committee.

The First District of the Jiangsu Provincial River Police Team 112

Chief Chen Formally Assumed Office Yesterday

Chen Zekuan, Chief of the First District of the Jiangsu Provincial River Police Team, was ordered to take over at the end of May and formally assumed his duties more than a month ago. Yesterday at 2:00 PM, he formally took the oath of office at the First District Office in Minhang. Invitations were sent out in advance to various sectors to visit. Yesterday, more than 200 guests arrived. The Jiangsu Provincial Department of Civil Affairs specially sent Yan Shenyu, the Magistrate of Shanghai County, to represent and supervise the oath. The circumstances of yesterday's ceremony are recorded separately below.

Order of Ceremony: (1) Playing music; (2) Paying the highest respect to the Party flag, the national flag, and the portrait of the Premier; (3) Taking the oath; (4) Admonitory speech by the supervisor; (5) Admonitory speech by General Commander Xiong; (6) Speeches by guests; (7) Speech by the District Chief in response; (8) Playing music; (9) Taking photos; (10) Tea and refreshments.

Ceremony Proceedings: Sentries were posted around the Minhang District Office, and a military band escorted the guests. A shallow-water warship and 20 gunboats were anchored on the banks of the Huangpu River, all flying flags. Party and national flags were also hung throughout the District Office. The ceremony hall was located to the left of the office. After the music was played, Chief Chen took the oath. The Chief's oath was: "I solemnly swear to abide by the Premier's will, obey the Party's doctrines, abide by the laws, and devote myself wholeheartedly to my duties. I will never waste a single penny, misuse a single person, engage in private gain or corruption, or accept bribes. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This I swear." Then, Mr. Yan Shenyu and others delivered speeches in succession. The meeting adjourned at 4:00 PM.

Mr. Yan's Admonitory Speech: Mr. Yan Shenyu delivered an admonitory speech, saying in essence: "Today is the ceremony for Chief Chen to formally take the oath of office. Shenyu is honored to be here representing the Department of Civil Affairs to participate in this grand ceremony. In general, every official must take an oath when taking office, but at the same time, the general public has a question, that is, whether they can fully implement their oath. Chief Chen's academic knowledge and experience are well known, and the importance of the Jiangsu River Police is also well known. Governance must have a good system and law. This is the matter of governing methods. However, with a good system and law, there must also be capable people to properly implement it. This is the matter of governing people. Therefore, Director Hu of the Department of Civil Affairs once said that without capable people, even with a good system and law, it would be useless. Moreover, the more laws there are, or the more precise they are, the more convenience it provides for those who engage in private gain and corruption. Now the Department of Civil Affairs has found capable people, such as Chief Chen, and entrusted him to fill this position. It is indeed a cause for celebration. Moreover, Shenyu also undertakes the governance of Shanghai, and especially feels that Shanghai County and the First District of the River Police have a close relationship. With Chief Chen in this position, he will definitely make a great contribution to defending the region. It is hot today, and I will not talk too much. I will express my hopes for Chief Chen. That is all."

Mr. Xiong's Admonitory Speech: Xiong Shihui, Commander-in-Chief of Bandit Suppression, represented Jiang Yi in delivering an admonitory speech, saying in essence: "Commander Xiong is unable to come here today due to an engagement, and specially commissioned his brother to represent him in participating in this grand ceremony. He feels very pleased. Commander Xiong entrusted me to state that he has two hopes for Chief Chen. The first point is that the content of the River Police has been complex in the past and should be reorganized, and should be diligently trained in advance to have discipline and education. The second point is that bandits and reactionary elements are constantly stirring. On land, there are regular army police and security teams to suppress them at any time. However, the rivers and streams in the Jiangnan area of Jiangsu Province are complicated, so the River Police must work hard to suppress them at any time so that the people can live and work in peace and contentment."

Speeches by Guests: Lu Quan, the Magistrate of Jinshan County, stated that after Chief Chen took office, he immediately sent police to cooperate with the army to suppress the large gang of bandits in Jinshan, and they were able to disperse. Therefore, he represented the people of Jinshan in thanking him and expressed his hope that he would continue to work hard, etc. In addition, representatives from the Shanghai County Party Department and the Jinshan County Party Department, as well as Commander Xiong from the Logistics Department of the Garrison Headquarters, also gave many speeches.

Mr. Chen's Response: Chief Chen delivered a speech in response, saying, "I am very sorry that the officials have graced us with their presence in this hot weather today. I was ordered to take this position, and it has been many days. I am only formally taking the oath of office today because at the beginning of my tenure, a large bandit disaster occurred in Jinshan. I first went on patrol myself and sent a fleet to suppress them, and at the same time requested assistance from the army. They have now been suppressed. However, I feel that the accumulated abuses of the River Police over the past few decades are too deep, and there is too little discipline. Therefore, I plan to start training them to become an elite force that will make it easier to suppress bandits. I have already submitted three requests to the Department of Civil Affairs: (1) to find ways to facilitate transportation; (2) to find ways to speed up communications; and (3) to find ways to expedite the transport of police teams. Once approved, they can be implemented. From now on, I will follow the provincial government's plan for bandit suppression and work hard to implement it."

Mr. Chen's Brief Biography: Chief Chen, whose courtesy name is Bohua, is 38 years old and a native of Wuxing, Zhejiang. He graduated from the Japanese Naval Academy and has served as an instructor at the Naval Headquarters, supervisor of students studying in Japan, consul stationed in Zhennampo, Japan, and secretary of the Songhu Garrison Headquarters.

Chen Zekuan Inspected Troops the Day Before Yesterday 113

After Chen, the Chief of the First District of the Jiangsu Provincial River Police Team, took office in May of this year and inspected the various teams, he saw that the morale of his troops was declining and the personnel were old and weak. Therefore, he seriously reorganized and rigorously carried out military training. In the past two months, the old appearance has been changed. Recently, in order to examine the training results of the various teams, on the day before the formal oath-taking ceremony (i.e., the 19th of this month), he transferred water patrols from the various teams to Minhang for joint exercises to be inspected. On that day, there were approximately 300 people. At 5:00 AM, the inspection was conducted at the Minhang Public Gymnasium, under the command of Zhu Chen, the captain of the Third Team. First, there was a military parade, then a divisional parade, followed by team exercises. Finally, Chief Chen gave an earnest speech. The officers and soldiers of each team were full of spirit, and their exercises were neat and tidy, especially the Third and Fourth Teams.

Director Wu of the Construction Bureau Inspects the Zhuji Line 114

Wu Wenhua, Director of the Construction Bureau of Shanghai County, was ordered by the Jiangsu Construction Department to inspect the Zhuhu County Road and to inspect the route from Zhujiajiao directly to Jiaxing in Zhejiang Province. It is said that a provincial road connecting Jiangsu and Zhejiang is planned to be built in the future to facilitate traffic between the two provinces. After receiving the order, Mr. Wu first went to Qingpu on the 16th of this month to inspect the Zhuhu County Road, and then met with Zhang Qiwo, Director of the Construction Bureau of the county, to inspect the Zhujia Line. The inspection has been completed and the report has been submitted to the Construction Department. According to Director Wu, the trip started from Qingcheng to Zhujiajiao, along the Gangshan Lake, and went west through Laitougang, Sanjinggang, Qichadang, Zhijiacun Village Gang, Lanlugang, Qingtiangang, Shitang, Xinyaoyuan, Liheinei Gang, and Laoheiyuan, for about 77 li. The Yuan Dang blocked the way and could not cross the river. He had no choice but to turn southwest, passing through Jinze Town to the corner of Yokohama Village to reach the boundary of Jiashan County in Zhejiang. Asked by scholars, if you want to go to Jiaxing, you must cross Jiashan, otherwise you must cross Yuan Dang and pass through Wujiang County to reach Jiaxing. However, the Yuan Dang River is very wide, and there are many white ponds along the road. The terrain is low-lying and construction will be very difficult in the future. Therefore, it is only convenient to reach Yokohama Village in Jiashan County, Zhejiang Province. Moreover, Yokohama is very close to the famous Xitang Town in Zhejiang Province, and transportation is even more convenient. Compared with reaching Zhejiang Province from Yuan Dang, it is more convenient. Although there are about 20 rivers in the middle, only the Sanjinggang and Lanlugang are larger rivers, and the others are small rivers. Even if you reach Zhejiang Province from Yuan Dang, you must pass through them.

Consultations on Maintaining Public Debt Methods 115

The National Public Debt Maintenance Association sent a letter to the Shanghai Bankers Association, saying, "Dear Sirs, in recent years, the market price of public debt treasury bills has plummeted, and the national economy is almost bankrupt. The banking funds are also showing signs of shaking. Your association, as the leader of the banks in Shanghai, has the responsibility to rescue and maintain it. We cannot stand by and watch it sink. We hereby put forward four urgent rescue measures, and we hope that you will hold a meeting as soon as possible to discuss and implement them. (1) Telegram the National Government to telegraphed the Shanghai Stock Exchange that all those who sell futures must prepay the cash to the Stock Exchange as collateral. All margin deposits need not be paid again. Those who are unable to prepay the cash will be treated as speculative short selling and refused to sell. Whether the cash is prepaid or not should be checked by government personnel stationed at the Stock Exchange to prevent abuses. (2) Telegram the Ministry of Finance to immediately order the Chief Inspector of Customs and the 2.5 Treasury Bill Committee to announce the debt fund on a ten-day basis and widely publish it in newspapers. At the same time, the Chief Inspector of Customs should be ordered to pre-allocate the 2.5 Treasury Bill Committee on a ten-day basis for the principal and interest due each month and deposit it in each bank for safekeeping in order to dispel rumors of the government withdrawing funds. (3) Consult with the banks in Shanghai. For all debt securities that the government repays principal and interest on time and has not defaulted, whether they are tariff, demobilization, or troop reduction debt, they should be allowed to be discounted separately and used as collateral. They should not be rejected on the grounds of hindering national credit. However, if the capital of each bank is insufficient and it cannot be used as collateral, it should be announced in advertisements that due to insufficient capital, any collateral will not be accepted from a certain month to a certain month. Only then will the debt securities be exempted from mortgage. If other types of collateral are accepted, but debt securities are rejected alone, they should be sued in court for destroying the credit of debt securities in order to warn against imitation. (4) The Central Bank, Bank of China, and Bank of Communications, which are acting as national treasuries, should abide by and implement the discounting of debt principal and interest coupons. All holders of principal and interest coupons should be allowed to discount them at a monthly interest rate of 4% for three months. After the three banks have implemented this for two weeks, all banks that issue banknotes must continue to implement it. After another two weeks, all banks that have not issued banknotes should also handle it uniformly and must not refuse. At the same time, a letter should be sent to the Ministry of Finance regarding the public debt fund, which should be allocated and stored in reasonable amounts to provide assistance. If the above four measures are implemented, the rumors that the government will withdraw funds and stop paying principal and interest will be dispelled. The interest rate on debt securities is extremely generous, with monthly interest rates all above 1% and around 2%. With the surplus cash in Shanghai, who would not want to rush to buy them at this time, and who would want to sell them at a discount and take losses? It is expected that within a month, customs tariffs, troop reduction, and demobilization debts can all rise to above 70%. This matter is of great importance to social finance and the banks themselves. Therefore, we are specially submitting measures in a letter for implementation. With best regards, the National Public Debt Maintenance Association."

Record of the Municipal Propaganda Conference 116

The Propaganda Department of the Shanghai Special Municipality Party Committee held its twelfth municipal propaganda conference at 3:00 PM yesterday. Recently, the Feng Army has shown signs of preparing for a general retreat. On the Jinpu Line, the Central Army abandoned Jinan in order to lure the enemy deep and annihilate them in one fell swoop. Therefore, the complete destruction of Shi You's Second Division was expected. Overall, the military situation is optimistic. Moreover, the Central Government's crusade against Yan and Feng this time is not about fighting for cities and expanding territories. The National Coal Production and Sales Association Submits a Document to the Government 117

Yu Shunqing, a member of the preparatory committee of the National Coal Production and Sales Association, submitted a document to the government, saying, "Submitting a request to rescue domestic coal, promote its use, and negotiate the recovery of property rights. I think that the decline of our country's industry and the depression of the people's livelihood are all due to the economic aggression of international imperialists and the shackles of unequal treaties. Taking the Fushun Coal Mine as an example, it is extremely heartbreaking. The Fushun coal area is under the jurisdiction of Ning Province and was originally our country's land and territory, which was never ceded to others. During the reign of Emperor Guangxu in the 27th year of Guangxu, Chinese people such as Wang Chengyao and others requested to raise funds for mining and named it the Huaxingli Coal Mining Company. After the Russo-Japanese War, Japan, taking advantage of its remaining prestige as a victorious country, falsely claimed that the mine was operated by Russians and forcibly occupied it. Although the Qing government negotiated with it repeatedly, it could not achieve anything. Later, due to the change of government in our country, the Japanese seized the opportunity to seize it for themselves, mining, transporting, and selling it without sparing any effort. The beginning and end of the process can be found in the case files. (Details are recorded separately.) All nationals should loudly call and collude to resist such great shame and humiliation in order to fulfill the duties of a national and save the right to benefit by one in ten thousand. However, there are unscrupulous and greedy merchants who recognize thieves as fathers, work as Japanese lackeys, and do everything possible to promote sales. They even go so far as to slander others with blood, exaggerating that no domestic coal can match the quality of Fushun coal. The Chinese people are not aware of this and are deceived by them. As a result, inferior goods flood the market and no one cares about domestic products. Not only that, the Customs only levies half tax on Fushun coal, while domestic coal is subject to heavy exploitation, such as the excessive miscellaneous taxes, increased train fares, and the military's occupation of carriages. Unequal treatment emerges one after another, causing the domestic coal market to be almost completely seized by foreigners, while domestic coal mines have goods piled up like mountains and cannot be sold. Factories are closed, merchants go bankrupt, and workers lose their jobs. All of these have a significant impact on the national economy. Over the years, the coal used in factories, ships, and trains in Shanghai, Wuhan, and across the country has mostly been Fushun coal. The facts are there and cannot be denied. According to the survey, approximately 7 million tons of Fushun miscellaneous coal are imported each year, and the rights overflow, worth 60 to 70 million yuan, which is a truly alarming number. We have always taken the promotion of domestic goods as our responsibility. Now that we have witnessed the endless seizure of foreigners and the indifference of merchants, we are worried and cannot remain silent. Therefore, we dare to submit a document and request that the Ministry of Finance be ordered to issue a notice to all customs offices to exempt or reduce the tax rate on domestic coal, cancel all harsh and detailed surcharges, and order the Ministry of Industry, Commerce, Communications, and Railways to issue a notice to all factories and transportation agencies across the country to promote domestic coal and not to disobey in public and obey in private, lose power and humiliate the country, and become a laughing stock for foreigners. We also hope to find ways to allocate vehicles and reduce transportation costs to benefit merchants and people, and order the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to investigate the case and recover the coal mining property rights that have been seized. This will not only be enough to save our declining domestic coal and encourage the interest of Chinese people in running industries, but also implement the will of our Party, our country, and our Premier to abolish unequal treaties. With all sincerity, we respectfully request your speedy implementation. We will be truly grateful for your public service. Respectfully submitted to the National Government."

French Concession Water and Electricity Employees to Join the Strike En Masse 119

Twelve Trolleys Operated Yesterday

French Authorities Maintain Strict Vigilance

The labor unrest at the French Concession Water and Electricity Company is expanding. As previously reported, the union held another general meeting yesterday afternoon. Details are as follows:

Meeting Details: The general meeting, originally scheduled to be held at the Public Sports Ground, was moved to the union hall due to the delay until 3 PM. The Municipal Party Department sent Zhang Huinian and Zhu Yakui as representatives to provide guidance. The Public Security Bureau ordered the police to maintain order. More than 800 workers, chaired by Xu Amei, proceeded with formalities. It was reported that since the Traffic Department joined the strike, the union's work has been extremely tense. Although the management remains stubborn and unrepentant, the entire workforce, due to the assistance of the Traffic Department workers, has gained fresh strength and is displaying extraordinary courage. They are determined to persevere in order to achieve their goals. It was also reported that three representatives from the Traffic Department had requested the assembly this morning not to take any action regarding the company's operation of trams today, and they would inquire about the company's terms. The three representatives then went to inquire.

Expansion of Operations: The original strike committee and picket line of the union were all composed of workers from the Mechanical Department. Now that workers from the Traffic Department have joined, these need to be expanded to facilitate active work. It is reported that the Traffic Department has nominated Mu Xiaoshan, Sun Aitang, Zhao Jinling, Wang Tiansan, and Yang Daoqing as members of the strike committee, and Wang Binglin, Guo Wenbin, Wang Xueren, Xu Asi, Wang Baofa, Gong Jinkun, Li Guanyi, Zhang Liansheng, Peng Xueshao, and Li Zhenyan as members of the picket line.

Chinese Staff Assistance: According to Xu Amei, the senior Chinese staff initially showed no indication during this strike. However, now that the matter has been prolonged without resolution, they also intend to join in solidarity with the workers. If the Chinese staff can unite and join, the company, which is currently in its billing period, has hundreds of thousands in outstanding accounts, which will definitely be affected, and the workers' victory can be predicted.

Reduced Number of Vehicles: Of the 56 vehicles in the French Concession Water and Electricity Company, only 12 were operated yesterday. These included eight Route 2 trams from Xujiahui to the 16th Pier, and four Route 10 trams from Lujiabang to the 16th Pier. If further damage occurs, it is feared that the number of vehicles will be further reduced today.

Expanded Support: During this strike, the Municipal Party Department has exerted its full effort to provide assistance. The support association organized by more than 60 groups is concerned that the strength of the support is still insufficient, so it has decided to expand it as much as possible to expedite the resolution.

Union Funds: Regarding the funding issue for the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers' Union, its monthly income used to be approximately 80 taels of silver, and the company also provided a monthly subsidy of 500 taels of silver. Since the strike, the company originally intended to suspend the subsidy, but through the efforts of, it was still paid as usual, and the July subsidy has also been received, so there should be absolutely no funding problems.

Arrested Workers: There have been repeated reports of workers being arrested. After discussion, the assembly yesterday resolved that if the above situation occurs again, the union will provide substantial assistance to the families of the arrested workers, providing them with funds to prevent panic and reassure the families of the arrested workers.

Company's New Workers: The company has not recruited many White Russians, but contracts were signed at the time of employment, so even if the workers return to work, these Russians may not pose a problem. As for the newly recruited Chinese workers, there are currently more than 200, but they are not familiar with the work, so the vehicles cannot be fully repaired. For this reason, the company is eager for the old workers to return to work, but they generally refuse to join out of righteous indignation.

Police Preparedness: The French Concession authorities have increased their vigilance yesterday. Each tram must have one Chinese and one Annamese constable. Each trailer has one Chinese constable. At each key intersection along the tram routes, there are French and Annamese constables patrolling in armed cars. The area around the headquarters at Lujiabang is even more heavily guarded. At the intersection of the Chinese concession and Luban Road, a dense network is set up, with only one person allowed to pass. Armed volunteer detectives are also stationed at various key points to prevent accidents. The iron gates at other locations such as the Old North Gate are all closed, and only one gate is left open at Dongxin Bridge to allow traffic to pass.

Various Unions Assist the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers 120

The support association for the French Concession Water and Electricity Workers held its first business committee meeting at 2 PM yesterday. Chen Peide, Zhao Zhenhui, Hu Shouqi, and others attended. The meeting proceeded with formalities. Hu Shouqi chaired, and Chen Peide recorded. The discussions included: (1) Set the date for the standing committee's regular meetings. (6) Appoint representatives to contact Chinese merchants for financial assistance to benefit the workers' livelihood. It was resolved to appoint Comrades Chen Peide, Lu Jingshi, and Li Yongxiang to make the contacts. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

The original text is recorded below: Shanghai Songhu Garrison Headquarters, Municipal Government, Local Court, Public Security Bureau, [Honorable officials], According to the letter from the Tongliyuan Leather Factory and Chengfa Leather Factory, which are invested in by overseas Chinese, (The submission has been seen in this newspaper on the 12th) etc. In response to this, Zhabei is located in the central area of northern Shanghai, with numerous military and police. This is of utmost importance. The Third Branch of the First District Pays Attention to Medical Issues 126

The third branch of the first district of this city held its 28th general meeting of party members yesterday. More than ten comrades attended. Representatives from the city, Qian Siqian, and representatives from the district, Ye Fei, attended to provide guidance. After performing the formalities, the discussion began. Five important cases were resolved: (1) Request the higher party department to forward to the municipal government to restrict the consultation fees of Chinese and Western doctors in this city: (A) The maximum outpatient fee should not exceed half a silver dollar. (B) The maximum house call fee should not exceed three silver dollars. (C) It is stipulated that the morning is for outpatient visits, the afternoon is for house calls, and after 10:00 PM is the time for "dialing" [emergency calls], and the house call fee can be doubled. (D) Within the outpatient hours each day, two hours should be set aside for sending poor patients for medical treatment, and a registration fee may be charged, but it should not exceed one dime of a small silver dollar. (E) Regardless of outpatient or house calls, in addition to the consultation fee already collected, no additional registration fees, transportation fees, etc. may be charged. (F) Cancel the registration restrictions to avoid missing anyone due to limited availability. The prices charged by the attached pharmacies should not differ too much from the original prices to benefit the poor patients. (2) Request the higher party department to forward to the municipal government to quickly establish municipal hospitals and pharmacies, which should be completely free for the poor patients. (3) Specify the locations of the tilting houses that should be demolished immediately, and report to the higher party department to forward to the municipal government, ordering the Public Works Bureau to demolish them quickly to benefit transportation. (4) Stipulate the methods for party members to report in groups at the party member assembly. (5) Stipulate the methods for Chinese medicine stores to carefully check the medicines they sell: (A) The name of the medicine must be stamped on the medicine wrapping paper. (B) After the medicine is dispensed, the person in charge of the pharmacy should carefully check it and stamp it on the prescription. (C) Order the doctors to write the names and quantities of the medicines on the prescription clearly, and not to be too perfunctory, so as to prevent the clerks from misreading and causing mistakes. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Strictly Prohibit the Use of Cuttlefish Traps for Fishing 128

The Shanghai County Government recently received instructions from the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Agriculture and Mining, roughly stating: "Approved the Construction Department's consultation stating that the North Sea Cuttlefish Industry General Representative Bao Yunzu has submitted a request to ban the use of cuttlefish traps for fishing in order to maintain livelihoods, etc. Please investigate and handle, etc. Approved the letter from the Zhejiang-Jiangsu Fisheries Affairs Bureau replying that the matter of cuttlefish traps for fishing has been ordered to be investigated and confirmed to be harmful to fish production, and it seems that it should be stopped and changed to net fishing to increase the production of cuttlefish, etc. The case was reviewed by the department. An investigation found that this cuttlefish trap fishing has restrictions or prohibitions on hindering the collection and capture of flora and fauna, as well as restrictions or prohibitions on fishing gear and fishing boats in the third paragraph of the same article. Strictly prohibit, etc." A proclamation was attached to the county. Yesterday, Magistrate Yan, in addition to ordering each district to comply with the regulations and prohibit them at any time, also issued and posted the proclamation, ordering all fishing households to be aware of it. After this notice, all cuttlefish fishing must change traps to nets. If there are any more cases of placing traps in the sea to catch cuttlefish, once discovered or reported, they will be severely punished and will not be pardoned.

Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau Proclaims Opium Cessation Measures 130

The Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau issued a proclamation yesterday, stating, "In accordance with the instructions of the Municipal Government No. 4787, it has been approved by the Opium Prohibition Committee to investigate the opening of hospitals that also handle opium cessation matters, and the establishment of municipal and county opium cessation centers. Opium addicts have been found and sent to hospitals to be forced to quit. It is feared that the general opium addicts do not fully understand the opium cessation measures and are afraid to move forward, which is a great loss of the central government's intention to set up opium cessation hospitals to encourage opium addicts to confess and quit opium. In accordance with Article 16 of the Opium Prohibition Implementation Regulations, all opium addicts who confess and are willing to be admitted to the hospital for opium cessation, or quit opium, before being discovered, are exempt from punishment. After deliberation at the 39th committee meeting, it was resolved to consult with each provincial government and each special municipal government to make announcements so that opium addicts will have the opportunity to confess and be admitted to the hospital to quit opium, etc. In addition to separate consultations, the relevant cases are consulted for reference and handling, and it is hoped that the subordinates will comply with the regulations, etc. In accordance with this, in addition to the external order, the bureau is ordered to comply with the regulations and jointly make announcements so that the opium addicts will be aware of this. All those who have this addiction are limited to applying to the opium cessation hospital on their own, so that they can fundamentally quit opium. If there are any who deliberately disobey, once discovered, they will be detained and severely punished, without leniency. Each should take heed and not violate. This announcement, (The following hospitals designated to handle opium cessation are listed) Shanghai Municipal Hospital, at Santai Wharf in the South City, China Red Cross General Hospital, Hague Road in the Concession, Southeast Hospital, in Hugunying, South City, Pingmin Hospital, Xinjiang Road in Zhabei, Jiangsu Opium Cessation Hospital, Zhizaoju Road in the South City, (Opium Cessation Fee Measures) Those who stay in first and second class wards, in addition to the hospital fees, the first class is 3.5 yuan per day, the second class is 2.4 yuan, the third class is 1.3 yuan, and a total of 10 yuan is collected for opium cessation fees. The fourth class ward only charges a hospital fee of 5 jiao per day, and the opium cessation fee is waived. For inpatient opium cessation, the first class costs 50 yuan in total, the second class costs 30 yuan in total, and the third class costs 15 yuan. The poor can request a reduction. Those who stay in the first class ward are charged 3 yuan for inpatient fees per day, and another 10 yuan for opium cessation fees. Those who stay in the second class ward are charged 2 yuan for inpatient fees per day, and another 8 yuan for opium cessation fees. Those who stay in the third class ward are charged 1 yuan for inpatient fees per day, and another 5 yuan for opium cessation fees. Inpatient meals cost 3 jiao per day. For those who have an addiction of one qian until opium cessation, a total of 10 yuan is charged for opium cessation fees. However, those who are truly unable to pay may request a reduction or exemption. Inpatient opium cessation costs 2 yuan per day for first class, 1.5 yuan for second class, 1 yuan for third class, and 7 jiao for fourth class. The truly poor may request a reduction or exemption. For outpatient opium cessation, the fee is 3 yuan per visit."

China First Credit Insurance Company Established 131

Credit insurance is extremely beneficial to society. Credit insurance companies in the United Kingdom were established earliest, approximately 200 years ago. The United States followed, and had credit insurance company organizations 70 years ago. Japan also imitated the United Kingdom and the United States to establish credit insurance companies 20 years ago, which is extremely convenient for society. Various personnel matters in society require credit as a guarantee, so those seeking employment must first find a guarantor. The difficulty of finding a guarantor is greater than seeking employment. Often, those who are new to society lack credit, and even if they have talents, it is difficult to find a suitable guarantor, so they cannot take up employment. Those who provide guarantees are also wary of the heavy responsibility and dare not act rashly. In the event of an accident, the guarantor may even go bankrupt. The employer is also greatly affected. Currently, several prominent figures in the Shanghai business community, recognizing that China does not yet have such a company, have jointly invested in establishing the China First Credit Insurance Company on Sichuan Road to alleviate this difficulty. After submitting a request to the Ministry of Industry and Commerce for approval and registration, a license was issued. The organization has been established. The company can provide guarantees for those who have obtained employment but cannot obtain a guarantor. The fees are extremely low, but the responsibility is extremely heavy. For those who are guaranteed by the company, the company is responsible for compensating the employer for all acts of fraud, theft, embezzlement, and malfeasance that cause the employer to suffer losses. This is an unprecedented innovation in China, which is of great benefit to society and individuals.

Liu Jiwen's Sued Case Still Requires Appeal 140

The Verdict of the Construction Contractor's Loss

This newspaper previously reported that the current Jianghai Customs Superintendent Liu Jiwen and Chen Yangjie were sued by construction contractor Lin De for non-payment of construction costs. The Special District Local Court ruled against the plaintiff, and Lin, dissatisfied, retained lawyers Zhang Deqin and Shen Yuesheng to file an appeal with the Second Branch of the Jiangsu High Court. The inquiry reveals that this dispute occurred while Superintendent Liu was the mayor of the Nanjing Special Municipality. The Special District Local Court believed that the case was not under the jurisdiction of the court, so it did not open the trial and immediately rejected the plaintiff's lawsuit. Now, the full text of the judgment is copied below to clarify the content of the case.

(Main text) The plaintiff's lawsuit is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. (Facts) The plaintiff sued the defendants for withholding construction fees of 2,000 yuan and failing to pay them, filing a lawsuit with the court. The statement stated that the plaintiff contracted to build construction projects for the Nanjing Municipal Government, and on April 15, the Nanjing Municipal Finance Bureau allocated various outstanding payments. The plaintiff's construction costs were also included in the allocation, amounting to 4,000 yuan. The funds were transferred by the Nanjing Municipal Engineering Bureau. When the plaintiff went to collect the construction fees, the first defendant suddenly ordered the director of the Municipal Engineering Bureau to withhold 2,000 yuan, so the Engineering Bureau only agreed to allocate 2,000 yuan. However, although the bureau paid 2,000 yuan, it still wanted the plaintiff to write a receipt for 4,000 yuan. At that time, the plaintiff thought that the first defendant would be discharged from the position of Nanjing mayor on April 19, and if the payment was not collected before the first defendant was discharged, it would inevitably involve more trouble in the future, so he painfully wrote a receipt for 4,000 yuan. After the plaintiff received 2,000 yuan, he was unclear about the reasons for withholding the money, so he went to the residence of the first defendant with the director of the Engineering Bureau to inquire about the reasons for withholding the money. At that time, he only said that it was withheld on behalf of the second defendant. Later, the plaintiff requested the first defendant to temporarily retain the withheld funds and asked the first defendant to personally write a receipt for the withheld funds of 2,000 yuan as proof. Unexpectedly, after the plaintiff returned to Shanghai, he repeatedly visited the second defendant but was refused to meet. The first defendant repeatedly corresponded but still instructed to negotiate with the second defendant, which was obviously a deliberate evasion. In desperation, this lawsuit was filed to pursue the matter. The plaintiff also submitted a photograph of a note for 2,000 yuan. The first defendant's address was filled in as the Jianghai Customs Superintendent's Office, and the second defendant's address was filled in as the office of the Great China Company. This court reviewed and made a judgment. (Reasons) Article 14 of the Civil Procedure Law states that the lawsuit shall be under the jurisdiction of the court where the defendant's ordinary trial registration is located. Article 15, paragraph 1, states that ordinary trial registration is determined by the address. Article 16, paragraph 1, states that the ordinary trial registration of the national treasury shall be determined according to the location of the agency representing the national treasury for litigation. The ordinary trial registration of all public corporations other than the national treasury shall be determined according to the location of its public affairs office. The money sued for by the plaintiff in this case is the construction price of the Nanjing Special Municipality construction project, and the location of the office and the public affairs office cannot be recognized as the defendant's ordinary trial registration. According to the above provisions, this case is not under the jurisdiction of this court. The plaintiff filed a lawsuit with this court, which is a jurisdictional error. According to Article 290, paragraph 1, item 1 of the Civil Procedure Law, it is rejected. The litigation costs shall be borne by the plaintiff. The judgment is specially made as the main text.

The Hairdresser's Apprentice Did Commit Violent Acts 141

Already Verified by the Forensic Doctor

Although Chen Lianying Was Defiled

But the Hymen Is Intact

Recently, cases of rape of young girls have occurred repeatedly, which is truly a worry for social customs and people's hearts. The Special District Local Court tried another similar case the day before yesterday. The matter has been published in this newspaper. The defendant is Zhou Zicai, a 17-year-old apprentice at the Kuifa Barber Shop at No. 440 North Henan Road. The young girl who was raped is Xiu Lian, the daughter of Mrs. Chen, a Guangdong woman living at No. 439 next door to the shop. She is eight years old. According to Zhang Tianyin, the lawyer for the Public Security Bureau, after this case occurred, the Hongkou Public Security Bureau sent detectives to the hospital for an examination. After the doctor issued an examination report, it stated that the girl had indeed been raped, but the hymen was still intact. The examination report was then submitted to the case. Subsequently, Mrs. Chen came to the case and confessed that on the afternoon of the 18th of this month, I went out to shop, and when I returned home after a while, my daughter Xiu Lian suddenly said to me that she had been beaten in the thighs by Zhou Zicai next door, and it was very painful now. I looked at her and saw that her skin was red. Later, I saw the girl walking unsteadily, and I was very suspicious. In the evening, when bathing her, I saw blood flowing from her private parts, so I strictly questioned her. The girl no longer denied it and began to say that after I went out, she was lured to the loft by Zhou, who took off her clothes and pants and committed indecent acts on her. The girl cried out in pain, and the defendant still did not stop his bestial behavior. I heard the girl's words, so I reported it to the Public Security Bureau, etc. When questioned, Zhou confessed that he was from Jiangbei and that Xiu Lian often came to my shop. On the afternoon of that day, she came again and went up to the loft. I once reached into her pants with my hand and touched her lower body, but I did not rape her, etc. Subsequently, according to Xiu Lian's confession, at that time, I went up to the loft, and Zhou first took off my pants, and then he also took off his pants, and then he committed rape. I screamed, and he slapped my cheeks. Judge Ge Zhitian, in order to prove whether rape had actually occurred, specially ordered the police to escort Zhou and Xiu Lian to the forensic examination room. After a detailed examination by the forensic doctor for a long time, the police brought the two people to the case, and the forensic doctor reported that two places on Xiu Lian's genitals were injured, but the hymen was still intact. Zhou Zicai's glans was red and swollen, and he did commit an act of adultery. The court then ordered the defendant to be detained and adjourned the hearing to another date and appointed a lawyer to defend the defendant so that he could enjoy legal benefits.

Mother-in-law and Landlord Are Suspicious

Liang Renkang Avoids Appearing in Court

Zhu Wanrong, 45 years old, from Zhenjiang, is currently a partner at the Shenchengcang Tea and Food Shop in Xiaodongmen. He is suing his wife, Jiang, for adultery with Liang Renkang, a firefighter's chauffeur. Jiang is 36 years old and married Zhu in September of the Xuantong year. She has one son, 12 years old. On January 1 of this year, he suddenly received a letter from his wife, Jiang, from Shanghai, which revealed her intention to divorce Zhu. Subsequently, according to the defendants Zhu and Jiang, after marrying Zhu, because Zhu liked gambling, she never received a penny from him. The family's expenses were always earned by my own hands. By the end of last year, I really could not afford the rent, so I moved to the Taifeng Old Iron Shop opened by my brother and stayed there temporarily. I did not know Liang, etc. Judge Sun instructed both parties to leave and adjourned the hearing for seven days to investigate further.

Difficult to Marry a Concubine with a Fierce Wife

Chen Yongqing, from Huzhou, is a sugar and dried goods peddler. He lives in Shijia Lane, Nanshi. Chen is 50 years old and has no children. Chen's wife was very angry and entrusted a neighbor to spend two yuan to secretly follow her husband to the place where he was hiding his lover. Not until the day before did she learn the address. The night before, she gathered her brothers and sisters and went to Tingyun Lane. After entering the house, she saw her husband and concubine having dinner. Xuefeng's father went to the Tingyun Lane address with his daughter yesterday and found that all the belongings were gone. He then contacted the matchmaker to negotiate with Chen, but it is unknown how it will be resolved.

Strange Tales of Youthful Swindlers 144

Young People Should Pay Attention

Recently, in Nanshi and other places, a kind of petty thief, about 20 years old, has been discovered. They suddenly have whimsical ideas to lure and deceive young children living at home. For those who are the same age as them, they design to coax and lure them, saying that hundreds of apprentices are wanted in a certain place. The monthly salary can be more than 40 yuan, and food and accommodation are provided. Don't miss such a good opportunity. If anyone is willing, our colleagues and I will be setting off, and you can also go with us. However, this matter cannot be told to parents, or they may obstruct it, and losing this benefit would be a pity. Unaware children mistakenly believe it to be true and all agree to follow. They even secretly take property from home and pool their travel expenses. When they arrive at the dock to meet him, he says that since you have collected your travel expenses, it is inconvenient to carry them on your body. Why not give them to me for safekeeping? At this time, the children trust him quite a bit, so they willingly give them to him. After boarding the ship, just as the ship is about to set sail, he takes advantage of the opportunity to sneak back to the dock with the money and flee without a trace. At this point, the children realize they have been deceived, but the ship has already set sail. It is too late to regret. Therefore, after arriving at the other port, they pawn their clothes for money and take a ship back to Shanghai, crying in vain. For example, on the 14th of this month, two sons, one from the Mou family on Xiaonanmen Street and the Zhao family in Yujia Lane, were lured to Ningbo by such people. Without relatives and no money, they ended up pawning their clothes for food and returning home. Afraid of their fathers and brothers scolding them, they did not return immediately. Lingering until they could no longer manage, they returned on a ship the day before yesterday. Their parents, who had been in a panic, were shocked to learn the truth after questioning their children. They could only sigh. The strangeness of the swindle is truly incomprehensible.

Eighty Bolts Sent to the Hotel

Obtained Money All the Way to the Bund

Attempted to Escape but Was Seized by a Friend

The Original Stolen Goods Were Not Found in the Hotel

Wu Yichang and Sun Jinsheng conspired with Li, who is on the run, on the 5th of this month to defraud the Huasi Ge Factory opened by Qu Jingdong in the French Concession of eighty bolts of Minghua Ge worth 774 yuan. After the case occurred, only Wu and Sun were arrested, but the original stolen goods had been taken away by their accomplice Li and had fled without a trace. The Public Security Bureau sent Wu and Sun to the French Court the day before yesterday to be investigated. The plaintiff complained about the previous situation, stating that the two defendants in the case came that day, pretending to be customers buying goods. At that time, they ordered eighty bolts of Minghua Ge and instructed them to send the goods to Room 73 of the Jiangdong Hotel in Xin Kaihe, Xiaodongmen, to collect the money. The merchant believed it to be true and sent partner Han Shiquan to deliver the goods. When he arrived at the hotel, Wu claimed that the goods had been placed in the hotel and took him to Dadongmen to collect the money. Han followed him. Unexpectedly, he went to Dadongmen, detoured through several places, and then went to the Bund, trying to escape. Therefore, he was seized by Han and taken to the Public Security Bureau, which sent detectives to the hotel to retrieve the stolen goods. Unexpectedly, it had been taken away by their accomplice Li, who had fled without a trace. Only the accomplice Sun Jinsheng was arrested and requested to be severely investigated. When questioned, Wu Qunchang admitted that the conspiracy was actually initiated by Li, who is on the run. Now the goods have been taken away by Li, who has fled. Sun Jinsheng confessed that although the people knew Wu, they did not dare to conspire to defraud. Judge Zhu sentenced Wu to three months in a Western prison and Sun to one month as a warning.

The standard contract for renting Nanshi wharves was drafted by the Port Authority and submitted to the Municipal Government for amendment and approval. Contracts will be signed with various shipping companies shortly. However, the rental fees for each wharf should be specified to be included in the contracts and to ensure compliance. It is learned that the Port Authority has separately determined the rental fees. Wharf No. 1 in Nanshi is over 64 meters long, with an excellent location, and the monthly rent is 1,500 national currency. Wharves No. 2 to No. 6 are the same length as No. 1 but slightly less favorable in location, each with a monthly rent of 1,300 yuan. Wharf No. 7 is the smallest, only about one-third of the above, with a monthly rent of 500 yuan. Wharves No. 8 and No. 9 are the same length and location as No. 2 to No. 6, each with a monthly rent of 1,300 yuan. Wharves No. 13 to No. 17 vary in length, from over 40 meters to over 60 meters, and are located south of the Customs House, each with a monthly rent of 1,200 yuan. In addition, Wharves No. 11, 12, and 18 are designated as public wharves, and fees are charged on a temporary basis according to the berthing fee regulations. Each wharf is estimated to collect about 1,000 yuan in berthing fees per month. The rental fees for the above fourteen wharves total over 250,000 yuan. It is reported that these regulations have been approved by the Municipal Government for record.

Zhou Shi Cancels Engagement Lawsuit 154

Zhou Cheng Yun (the niece of Zhou Wanpeng, the former chief of the telegraph bureau) of Dachang Town, Baoshan, has a third daughter named Wen Lan. In the twelfth year of the Republic [1923], Sun Wenzhen introduced her to Shi Weigao's son, Lixun, for marriage. However, Lixun demanded that Zhou's daughter continue her studies and graduate from elementary school. However, Zhou Cheng Yun said that all his daughters had only graduated from primary school, and he could not make an exception for his third daughter. Despite repeated persuasion from the matchmaker and friends, there was no result. Last spring, Shi Lixun wrote to Zhou's father, saying that if she did not go to school as agreed, he would cancel the engagement. As a result, misunderstandings arose. Later, Shi's father set a date for the wedding and personally went to Zhou's father to apologize. However, Zhou strongly opposed Shi's request and hired lawyer Yu Congdao to sue the Local Court for damages. Shi also hired lawyers Wang Zengxian and Yuan Xilian to counterclaim for the return of the betrothal gifts. The case was heard in court by Judge Zhang Jinjian on the morning of the day before yesterday. Shi's son was absent due to illness, but all others were present. After the judge questioned Zhou's father and daughter and Shi Weigao to clarify the facts, he advised them to reconcile. Zhou Cheng Yun said that his daughter had to make her own decision. Zhou Wenlan said that she did not want to marry Shi Lixun because she had already sent a letter of cancellation. However, Shi Weigao said that he did not want to cancel the engagement. If Zhou Wenlan insisted on canceling, she would have to return the betrothal gifts and compensate for the losses. The judge ruled that reconciliation was impossible and ordered the debate to begin. Lawyer Yu, representing the plaintiff, stated that the cancellation had been made by Shi Lixun in his letter and that Zhou Wenlan had agreed. What they were now requesting was compensation for losses such as the cost of the banquet, totaling 300 yuan, and 800 yuan for emotional distress. Lawyer Wang, representing the defendant, argued that the cancellation required a procedure. The simplest was for the man to return the engagement card and the woman to return the betrothal gifts. In this case, the engagement had not been legally canceled, so how could they directly seek compensation for losses? Shi Lixun's letter was intended to urge Zhou Wenlan to study. The plaintiff had confiscated the material gifts, which were of value, but had not attached importance to the engagement card, which was of great significance to the woman, and had not sought its return, which was inconsistent with the law and human feelings and should be rejected. The case was judged yesterday. The plaintiff's claim for damages and the defendant's counterclaim for the return of the betrothal gifts were both rejected.

Continued Report on the Minsheng Canal Project in Qixian 164

The Jishiang Canal sluices and other projects of the Chinese Jishiang Canal of Henan Province in Qixian have been completed. Now we have received a letter from Mr. Dong Xiangqu, who initiated the project in Qixian. A few months ago, the Henan Provincial Relief Association sent Mr. Liu Xuxin to Qixian to inspect the canal project. He was very satisfied with the large-scale, cost-effective, and highly profitable project. The large stone bridge of the canal's dam was too large and required extra processing and materials, which slightly increased the cost. The project has recently been completed, but there are still unpaid wages that are urgently needed. The local area is barren and there is no way to borrow money. Therefore, the association was asked to borrow 2,000 yuan, which would be repaid after the autumn harvest. The association agreed that this large-scale project was beneficial to the people and approved the loan of 2,000 yuan to meet the urgent need. The funds have been remitted in full for urgent use.

Qiu Mingjiu, the magistrate of Baoshan County, received instructions from the Civil Affairs Department of Jiangsu Province the day before yesterday, stating that district heads in various counties who were weak in ability and improper in their actions would be transferred to the province for retraining. Officials have been sent to various counties for inspection and factual reporting is required. Lu Fengpu, the head of the second district of the county, has been repeatedly accused by local people and has accumulated many cases.
